<division>Guide to Division&#160;208</division>

Table of sections

208-5	What is an exempting entity?
 208-10	Former exempting entities
 208-15	Distributions by exempting entities and former exempting entities

208-5  What is an exempting entity?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An exempting entity is a corporate tax entity that is effectively owned by

entities that, either because they are not Australian residents or because they

receive distributions as exempt income, would not be able to fully utilise

franking credits on distributions by the corporate tax entity.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>In deciding whether a corporate tax entity is effectively owned by such entities, these rules: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>look at the membership interests in the entity that involve the holder of

the interest in bearing the risks and accruing the opportunities of ownership

of the entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ask whether at least 95% of those membership interests, and 95% of any

interests in those membership interests, are held by Australian residents or

entities that receive distributions as exempt income.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

208-10  Former exempting entities

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		When an entity ceases to be an exempting entity, it becomes a former

exempting entity.

 </dl></dl>

208-15  Distributions by exempting entities and former exempting entities

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		To ensure that franking credits accumulated by an exempting entity are not

the target of franking credit trading, these rules:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>limit the circumstances in which a distribution franked with those credits

can give rise to benefits under the imputation system; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>quarantine those credits by moving them into a separate account, called

the exempting account, when the entity ceases to be an exempting entity; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>deny a recipient of a distribution franked with a credit from that account

any benefit under the imputation system as a result of that distribution,

unless the recipient was a member of the entity immediately before it became a

former exempting entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;208-A&#151;What are exempting entities and former exempting entities?

Table of sections

208-20	Exempting entities
 208-25	Effective ownership of entity by prescribed persons
 208-30	Accountable membership interests
 208-35	Accountable partial interests
 208-40	Prescribed persons
 208-45	Persons who are taken to be prescribed persons
 208-50	Former exempting companies

208-20  Exempting entities

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity is an _exempting entity_ at a

particular time if, at that time, the entity is effectively owned by prescribed

persons.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Prescribed persons are identified in sections&#160;208-40

and 208-45.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

208-25  Effective ownership of entity by prescribed persons

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An entity is _effectively owned by prescribed persons_ at a

particular time if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at that time:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>not less than 95% of the <sup>*</sup>accountable membership interests in

the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>not less than 95% of the <sup>*</sup>accountable partial interests in the

entity;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		are held by, or held indirectly for the benefit of, prescribed persons; or

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>paragraph&#160;(a) does not apply but it would nevertheless be reasonable

to conclude that, at that time, the risks involved in, and the opportunities

resulting from, holding accountable membership interests, or accountable

partial interests, in the entity that are not held by, or directly or

indirectly for the benefit of, prescribed persons are substantially borne by,

or substantially accrue to, prescribed persons.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In deciding whether it would be reasonable to conclude as mentioned in

paragraph&#160;(1)(b):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>have regard to any <sup>*</sup>arrangement in respect of

<sup>*</sup>membership interests (including unissued membership interests), or

in respect of <sup>*</sup>partial interests, in the entity (including any

derivatives held or issued in connection with those membership interests or

partial interests) of which the entity is aware; but</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>do not have regard to risks involved in the ownership of membership

interests, or partial interests, in the entity that are substantially borne by

any person in the person's capacity as a secured creditor.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An entity has a _partial interest_ in a <sup>*</sup>corporate

tax entity if it has an interest in a <sup>*</sup>membership interest in the

corporate tax entity.

</dd> </dl></dl>

208-30  Accountable membership interests

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The purpose of this section is to identify which <sup>*</sup>membership

interests in an entity are relevant in determining whether the entity is

effectively owned by prescribed persons.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>membership interest in an entity is an _accountable membership interest_ if it is not an excluded membership interest.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>membership interest in an entity is an _excluded membership interest_ if, having regard to: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the purposes for which the membership interest was issued; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any special or limited rights connected with, arising from, or attached to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the membership interest; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>other membership interests in the entity held by the holder of the

membership interest; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>membership interests in the entity held by persons other than the holder

of the membership interest; or</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>interests in any of the above;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		including rights that are conferred or exercisable only if the holder of the

membership interest or interests concerned is, or is not, a prescribed person;

and

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the extent to which any such special or limited rights are similar to or

differ from the rights that are normally attached to the ownership of

<sup>*</sup>ordinary membership interests in <sup>*</sup>corporate tax

entities; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the relationship between the value of the membership interest and the

value of the entity; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>any relationship or connection (whether of a personal or business nature)

between holders of membership interests in the entity of which the entity is

aware; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>any <sup>*</sup>arrangement in respect of membership interests (including

unissued membership interests) in the entity, or interests in membership

interests in the entity, of which the entity is aware;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

it would be reasonable to conclude that the membership interest is not relevant in determining whether the entity is effectively owned by prescribed persons because holding the membership interest does not involve the holder bearing the risks, or result in the accrual to the holder of the opportunities, of ownership of the entity that ordinarily arise from, or are ordinarily attached to, the holding of ordinary membership interests in an entity.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>In applying subsection&#160;(3), the fact that a person is a trustee is to

be disregarded.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>Without limiting subsection&#160;(3), a <sup>*</sup>membership interest in an entity held by a person who is not a prescribed person is an _excluded membership interest_ if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>it is a finance membership interest; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>it is a distribution access membership interest; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>it does not carry the right to receive distributions; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>it was issued, transferred or acquired for a purpose (other than an

incidental purpose) of ensuring that the entity is not effectively owned by

prescribed persons.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>membership interest is a _finance membership interest_ if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the membership interest is a <sup>*</sup>non-equity share in the entity;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>having regard to the rights attached to the membership interest and to any

<sup>*</sup>arrangement with respect to the membership interest of which the

entity is aware, the membership interest is equivalent to a debt owed by the

entity to the holder of the membership interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>membership interest to which subsection&#160;(6) does not

apply is a _finance membership interest_ if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the manner in which the <sup>*</sup>distributions payable in respect of

the membership interest are calculated, and the conditions applying to the

payment of such distributions, indicate that the distributions paid are

equivalent to the receipt by the person to whom they are paid of interest or an

amount in the nature of or similar to interest; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the capital invested by the holder of the membership interest will be

redeemed or, because of an <sup>*</sup>arrangement between the holder and the

entity or an <sup>*</sup>associate of the entity, it is reasonable for the

holder to expect that the capital will be redeemed, for an amount that is not

less than, or for property (including other membership interests in the entity)

the value of which is not less than, the amount paid for the membership

interest; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the membership interest is redeemable by the entity by payment of a lump

sum or by the transfer of property, or the membership interest has a preferred

right to a repayment of capital on a winding up, where the amount of the lump

sum or the value of the property, or the amount of the capital to be repaid, as

the case may be, is to be calculated by reference to an implicit interest rate.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>membership interest in an entity is a _distribution access membership interest_ if, having regard to:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the terms of the issue of the membership interest, including any guarantee

of payment of distributions; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amounts of the <sup>*</sup>distributions paid on the membership

interest relative to the issue price of the membership interest; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>whether there is any guaranteed rate at which <sup>*</sup>franked

distributions are to be paid on the membership interest; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the duration of the period within which the membership interest was

issued; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the rights attached to other membership interests in the entity; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>any other relevant matters;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

it could be concluded that the membership interest was issued only for the purpose of paying distributions to the holder of the membership interest.

208-35  Accountable partial interests

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The purpose of this section is to identify which <sup>*</sup>partial

interests in an entity are relevant in determining whether the entity is

effectively owned by prescribed persons.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>partial interest in an entity is an _accountable partial interest_ if it is not an excluded partial interest.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>partial interest in an entity is an _excluded partial interest_ if, having regard to: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the purposes for which the interest was granted; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the nature of the interest; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any special or limited rights connected with or arising from:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the interest; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>other <sup>*</sup>membership interests, or partial interests, in the

entity held by the holder of the interest; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>membership interests, or partial interests, in the entity held by

persons other than the holder of the interest;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		including rights that are conferred or exercisable only if the holder of the

membership interests or partial interests concerned is, or is not, a prescribed

person; and

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the extent to which the interest is similar to or differs from beneficial

ownership; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the relationship between the value of the interest and the value of the

entity; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>any relationship or connection (whether of a personal or business nature)

between holders of partial interests in the entity, and the holders of

membership interests in the entity, of which the entity is aware; and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>any <sup>*</sup>arrangement in respect of membership interests (including

unissued membership interests) in the entity, or partial interests in the

entity, of which the entity is aware;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

it would be reasonable to conclude that the partial interest is not relevant in determining whether the entity is effectively owned by prescribed persons because holding the membership interest to which the partial interest relates does not involve the holder bearing the risks, or result in the accrual to the holder of the opportunities, of ownership of the entity that ordinarily arise from, or are ordinarily attached to, the holding of <sup>*</sup>ordinary membership interests in an entity.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>In applying subsection&#160;(3), the fact that a person is a trustee is to

be disregarded.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>Without limiting subsection&#160;(3), a <sup>*</sup>partial interest in an entity is also an _excluded partial interest_ if it was granted or otherwise created, or was transferred or acquired, for a purpose (other than an incidental purpose) of ensuring that the entity is not effectively owned by prescribed persons. </dd> </dl></dl>

208-40  Prescribed persons

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A company is a _prescribed person_ in relation to another

<sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company is not an <sup>*</sup>Australian resident; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>were the company to receive a <sup>*</sup>distribution made by the other

corporate tax entity, the distribution would be <sup>*</sup>exempt income of

the company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A trustee is a _prescribed person_ in relation to a

<sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>all the beneficiaries in the trust are prescribed persons under other

provisions of this section; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>were the trustee to receive a <sup>*</sup>distribution made by the

corporate tax entity, the distribution would be <sup>*</sup>exempt income of

the trust estate.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>partnership is a _prescribed person_ in relation

to a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>all the partners are prescribed persons under other provisions of this

section; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>were the partnership to receive a <sup>*</sup>distribution made by the

corporate tax entity, the distribution would be <sup>*</sup>exempt income of

the partnership.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>An individual (other than a trustee) is a prescribed person in relation to

a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>he or she is not an <sup>*</sup>Australian resident; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>were he or she to receive a <sup>*</sup>distribution made by the corporate

tax entity, the distribution would be <sup>*</sup>exempt income of the

individual.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The Commonwealth, each of the States, the Australian Capital Territory,

the Northern Territory and Norfolk Island are prescribed persons in relation to

any <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity.

</dd> </dl></dl>

208-45  Persons who are taken to be prescribed persons

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section applies to a person that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is a <sup>*</sup>company, a trustee, or a <sup>*</sup>partnership, that

holds <sup>*</sup>membership interests (whether <sup>*</sup>accountable

membership interests or excluded membership interests), or <sup>*</sup>partial

interests (whether <sup>*</sup>accountable partial interests or excluded

partial interests), in a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity (the _relevant entity_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is not a prescribed person under section&#160;208-40.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>company that holds <sup>*</sup>membership interests, or

<sup>*</sup>partial interests, in the relevant entity is taken to be a

_prescribed person_ in relation to the relevant entity if the risks

involved in, and the opportunities resulting from, holding the membership

interests or partial interests are substantially borne by, or substantially

accrue to, as the case may be, one or more prescribed persons.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A trustee of a trust who holds <sup>*</sup>membership interests, or <sup>*</sup>partial interests, in the relevant entity is taken to be a _prescribed person_ in relation to the relevant entity if the risks involved in, and the opportunities resulting from, holding the membership interests or partial interests are substantially borne by, or substantially accrue to, as the case may be, one or more prescribed persons.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>A trustee of a trust who holds <sup>*</sup>membership interests, or <sup>*</sup>partial interests, in the relevant entity is taken to be a _prescribed person_ in relation to the relevant entity if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>unless subsection&#160;(7) applies, the trust is controlled by one or more

persons who are prescribed persons; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>all the beneficiaries who are presently entitled to, or during the

relevant year of income become presently entitled to, income from the trust are

prescribed persons.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>In determining whether subsection&#160;(3) or (4) applies in respect of a

trust that is controlled by a person, have regard to the way in which the

person, or any <sup>*</sup>associate of the person, exercises powers in

relation to the trust.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person _controls a trust_ if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has the power, either directly, or indirectly through one or

more interposed entities, to control the application of the income, or the

distribution of the property, of the trust; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person has the power, either directly, or indirectly through one or

more entities, to appoint or remove the trustee of the trust; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person has the power, either directly, or indirectly through one or

more entities, to appoint or remove beneficiaries of the trust; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the trustee of the trust is accustomed or under an obligation, whether

formal or informal, to act according to the directions, instructions or wishes

of the person or of an <sup>*</sup>associate of the person.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>Paragraph&#160;(4)(a) does not apply in relation to a trust if some of the

beneficiaries receiving income from the trust are not prescribed persons and

the Commissioner considers that it is reasonable to conclude that the risks

involved in, and the opportunities resulting from, holding the

<sup>*</sup>membership interests or <sup>*</sup>partial interests in the

relevant entity are substantially borne by, or substantially accrue to, as the

case may be, one or more persons who are not prescribed persons.</dd> <dt>(8)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>partnership that holds <sup>*</sup>membership interests, or <sup>*</sup>partial interests, in the relevant entity is taken to be a _prescribed person_ in relation to the relevant entity if the risks involved in, and the opportunities resulting from, holding the membership interests or partial interests are substantially borne by, or substantially accrue to, as the case may be, one or more prescribed persons.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>If any of the prescribed persons referred to in subsection&#160;(2), (3), <dt>(4)</dt><dd>or (8) is a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity, that subsection applies even if the risks involved in, and the opportunities resulting from, holding any of the <sup>*</sup>membership interests, or <sup>*</sup>partial interests, in that entity are substantially borne by, or substantially accrue to, as the case may be, one or more persons who are not prescribed persons. </dd></dd> </dl></dl>

208-50  Former exempting companies

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subject to subsection&#160;(2), a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity is a

_former exempting entity_ if it has, at any time, ceased to be an

<sup>*</sup>exempting entity and is not again an exempting entity.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If an entity that, at any time, becomes effectively owned by prescribed persons ceases to be so effectively owned within 12 months after that time, the entity is not taken, by so ceasing, to become a former exempting entity. </dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;208-B&#151;Franking with an exempting credit
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;208-B
 208-55  What this Subdivision is about

If a former exempting entity makes a distribution in circumstances where it could be franked, the entity can frank the distribution with an exempting credit.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

208-60	Franking with an exempting credit

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 208-60  Franking with an exempting credit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An entity _franks_ a <sup>*</sup>distribution _with an exempting credit_ if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity is a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity when the distribution

is made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity is a <sup>*</sup>franking entity that satisfies the

<sup>*</sup>residency requirement when the distribution is made; and</dd>

(c)	the distribution is a <sup>*</sup>frankable distribution; and

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity allocates an <sup>*</sup>exempting credit to the distribution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The residency requirement for an entity making a

distribution is set out in section&#160;202-20.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;208-C&#151;Amount of the exempting credit on a distribution
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;208-C
 208-65  What this Subdivision is about

<center>Back to Top</center>

The amount of the exempting credit on a distribution is that stated in the distribution statement, unless the amount stated exceeds the maximum franking credit for the distribution. In that case, it is nil.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

208-70	Amount of the exempting credit on a distribution

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 208-70  Amount of the exempting credit on a distribution

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subject to subsection&#160;(2), the amount of the <sup>*</sup>exempting

credit on a <sup>*</sup>distribution is that stated in the

<sup>*</sup>distribution statement for the distribution.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the sum of the <sup>*</sup>franking credit and the <sup>*</sup>exempting credit stated in the <sup>*</sup>distribution statement for a <sup>*</sup>distribution exceeds the <sup>*</sup>maximum franking credit for the distribution, the amount of the exempting credit on the distribution is taken to be nil. </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the franking credit stated in the distribution statement

exceeds the maximum franking credit for the distribution, the amount of the

franking credit on the distribution is taken to equal that maximum under

section&#160;202-65.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;208-D&#151;Distribution statements
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;208-D
 208-75  Guide to Subdivision&#160;208-D

Former exempting entities and exempting entities that make certain distributions must provide additional information in the distribution statement given to the recipient.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

208-80	Additional information to be included by a former exempting entity or exempting entity

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 208-80  Additional information to be included by a former exempting entity or exempting entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity that makes a

<sup>*</sup>distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with an exempting credit must

include in the <sup>*</sup>distribution statement given to the recipient, a

statement that there is an <sup>*</sup>exempting credit of a specified amount

on the distribution.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>exempting entity that makes a <sup>*</sup>frankable distribution to a <sup>*</sup>member must include in the <sup>*</sup>distribution statement given to the member, a statement to the effect that members who are <sup>*</sup>Australian residents are not entitled to a <sup>*</sup>tax offset or <sup>*</sup>franking credit as a result of the distribution, except for certain <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entities, and employees who receive the distribution in connection with certain <sup>*</sup>employee share schemes.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If, under subsection&#160;(1) or (2), a statement must be included in a <sup>*</sup>distribution statement, the distribution statement is taken not to have been given unless the statement is included. </dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;208-E&#151;Distributions to be franked with exempting credits to the same extent
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;208-E
 208-85  What this Subdivision is about

All frankable distributions made within a franking period must be franked to the same extent with an exempting credit.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

208-90	All frankable distributions made within a franking period must be franked to the same extent with an exempting credit
 208-95	Exempting percentage
 208-100	Consequences of breaching the rule in section&#160;208-90

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 208-90  All frankable distributions made within a franking period must be franked to the same extent with an exempting credit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an entity <sup>*</sup>franks a <sup>*</sup>distribution with an

exempting credit, it must frank each other <sup>*</sup>frankable distribution

made within the same <sup>*</sup>franking period with an exempting credit

worked out at the same <sup>*</sup>exempting percentage.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If an entity is not a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity for the whole of a <sup>*</sup>franking period (the _longer period_), then, for the purposes of subsection&#160;(1), each period within that longer period during which the entity is a former exempting entity is taken to be a _franking period_. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

208-95  Exempting percentage

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The _exempting percentage_ for a <sup>*</sup>frankable

distribution is worked out using the formula:

 </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1208.gif)</sub>

208-100  Consequences of breaching the rule in section&#160;208-90

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If an entity <sup>*</sup>franks a <sup>*</sup>distribution with an exempting

credit in breach of section&#160;208-90:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that distribution is taken not to have been franked with an exempting

credit; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each other <sup>*</sup>frankable distribution made by the entity within

the relevant <sup>*</sup>franking period is taken not to have been franked with

an exempting credit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;208-F&#151;Exempting accounts and franking accounts of exempting entities and former exempting entities
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;208-F
 208-105  What this Subdivision is about

This Subdivision:

*	creates an exempting account for each former exempting entity; and

*	identifies when exempting credits and debits arise in those accounts and the amount of those credits and debits; and

*	identifies when there is an exempting surplus or deficit in the account; and

*	identifies when franking credits and debits arise in the franking account of an entity because it is an exempting entity, or former exempting entity.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

208-110	Exempting account
 208-115	Exempting credits
 208-120	Exempting debits
 208-125	Exempting surplus and deficit
 208-130	Franking credits arising because of status as exempting entity or former exempting entity
 208-135	Relationships that will give rise to a franking credit under item&#160;5 of the table in section&#160;208-130
 208-140	Membership of the same effectively wholly-owned group
 208-145	Franking debits arising because of status as exempting entity or former exempting entity
 208-150	Residency requirement
 208-155	Eligible continuing substantial member
 208-160	Distributions that are affected by a manipulation of the imputation system
 208-165	Amount of the exempting credit or franking credit arising because of a distribution franked with an exempting credit
 208-170	Where a determination under paragraph 177EA(5)(b) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ affects part of the distribution
 208-175	When does a distribution franked with an exempting credit flow indirectly to an entity?
 208-180	What is an entity's share of the exempting credit on a distribution?
 208-185	Minister may convert exempting surplus to franking credit of former exempting entity previously owned by the Commonwealth

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 208-110  Exempting account

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Each <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity has an _exempting account_.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>
  Exempting surplus and deficit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An entity's <sup>*</sup>exempting account is in _surplus_ at a

particular time if, at that time, the sum of the <sup>*</sup>exempting credits

in the account exceeds the sum of the <sup>*</sup>exempting debits in the

account. The amount of the _exempting surplus_ is the amount of the

excess.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An entity's <sup>*</sup>exempting account is in _deficit_ at a particular time if, at that time, the sum of the <sup>*</sup>exempting debits in the account exceeds the sum of the <sup>*</sup>exempting credits in the account. The amount of the _exempting deficit_ is the amount of the excess. </dd> </dl></dl>

</tr></table><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Item&#160;9 is designed to reverse out franking debits that

arise in relation to a period during which the entity is an exempting entity.

The entity will receive an exempting debit instead.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

208-135  Relationships that will give rise to a franking credit under item&#160;5 of the table in section&#160;208-130

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A relationship between an entity making a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution

and the recipient of the distribution is of a type that gives rise to a

<sup>*</sup>franking credit under item&#160;5 or 6 of the table in

section&#160;208-130 if either:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>both entities are members of the same effectively wholly-owned group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the recipient holds more than 5% of the <sup>*</sup>membership interests

in the entity making the distribution (other than finance membership interests

or distribution access membership interests within the meaning of

section&#160;208-30 or membership interests that do not carry the right to

receive distributions) and it would be reasonable to conclude that the risks

involved in, and the opportunities resulting from, holding those membership

interests are substantially borne by, or substantially accrue to, the recipient.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In deciding whether it would be reasonable to make the conclusion

mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>have regard to any <sup>*</sup>arrangement in respect of the

<sup>*</sup>membership interests (including unissued membership interests) in

the entity making the distribution (including derivatives held or issued in

connection with those membership interests); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>do not have regard to risks involved in the ownership of membership

interests in the entity making the distribution that are substantially borne by

any person in the person's capacity as a secured creditor.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

208-140  Membership of the same effectively wholly-owned group

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Two <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entities are members of the _same effectively wholly-owned group of entities_ on a particular day if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>throughout that day, not less than 95% of the <sup>*</sup>accountable

membership interests in each of the entities, and not less than 95% of the

<sup>*</sup>accountable partial interests in each of the entities, are held by,

or are held indirectly for the benefit of, the same persons; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>paragraph&#160;(a) does not apply but it would nevertheless be reasonable

to conclude, having regard to the matters mentioned in subsection&#160;(2),

that, throughout that day, the risks involved in, and the opportunities

resulting from, holding accountable membership interests, or accountable

partial interests, in each of the entities are substantially borne by, or

substantially accrue to, the same persons.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The matters to which regard is to be had as mentioned in

paragraph&#160;(1)(b) are:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any special or limited rights attaching to <sup>*</sup>accountable

membership interests, or <sup>*</sup>accountable partial interests, in each of

the entities held by persons other than the persons mentioned in

paragraph&#160;(1)(b) or their <sup>*</sup>associates; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any special rights attaching only to accountable membership interests, or

accountable partial interests, in each of the entities held by the persons

mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) or their associates; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the respective proportions:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>that accountable membership interests in each of the entities held by the

persons mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) or their associates, and other

accountable membership interests in the entity concerned, bear to all the

accountable membership interests in that entity; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>that accountable partial interests in each of the entities held by the

persons mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) or their associates, and other

accountable partial interests in the entity concerned, bear to all the

accountable partial interests in that entity; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the respective proportions that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the total value of accountable membership interests in each of the

entities held by the persons mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) or their

associates, and the total value of other accountable membership interests in

the entity concerned, bear to the total value of all the accountable membership

interests in that entity; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the total value of accountable partial interests in each of the entities

held by the persons mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) or their associates, and

the total value of other accountable partial interests in the entity concerned,

bear to the total value of all the accountable partial interests in that

entity; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the purposes for which accountable membership interests, or accountable

partial interests, in each of the entities were issued or granted to persons

other than the persons mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) or their associates;

and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>any <sup>*</sup>arrangement in respect of accountable membership

interests, or accountable partial interests, in each of the entities held by

persons other than the persons mentioned in paragraph&#160;(1)(b) or their

associates (including any derivatives held or issued in connection with those

membership interests or interests) of which the entity concerned is aware.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

208-145  Franking debits arising because of status as exempting entity or former exempting entity

franking credits that arise in relation to a period during which the entity is

an exempting entity. The entity will receive an exempting credit instead. Note 2:	Item&#160;5 of the table is designed to reverse out franking credits that arise under the core rules because an entity receives a franked distribution from an exempting entity. Only a recipient who is itself an exempting entity is entitled to a franking credit in these circumstances.  </dl></dl>

208-150  Residency requirement

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The tables in sections&#160;208-115, 208-120, 208-130 and 208-145 are

relevant for the purposes of subsection 205-25(1).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection 205-25(1) sets out the residency requirement

for an income year in which, or in relation to which, an event specified in one

of the tables occurs. Note 2:	Section&#160;207-75 sets out the residency requirement that must be satisfied by the entity receiving a distribution when the distribution is made.  </dl></dl>

208-155  Eligible continuing substantial member

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>member of a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity is an

_eligible continuing substantial member_ in relation to a

<sup>*</sup>distribution made by the entity if the following provisions

apply.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>At both the time when the <sup>*</sup>distribution was made, and the time immediately before the entity ceased to be an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity, the <sup>*</sup>member was entitled to not less than 5% of: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>where the entity is a <sup>*</sup>company:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the voting shares (as defined in the _Corporations Act 2001_) in

the relevant former exempting entity are not divided into classes&#151;those voting

shares; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if the voting shares (as so defined) in the relevant former exempting

entity are divided into 2 or more classes&#151;the shares in one of those classes;

and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>where the entity is a <sup>*</sup>corporate unit trust or

<sup>*</sup>public trading trust&#151;the units in the trust; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>where the entity is a <sup>*</sup>corporate limited partnership&#151;the

income of the partnership.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>At both the time when the <sup>*</sup>distribution was made, and the time

immediately before the entity ceased to be an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity, the

<sup>*</sup>member was a person referred to in one or more of the following

paragraphs:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person who is not an <sup>*</sup>Australian resident;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>life insurance company;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an exempting entity;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>a trustee of a trust in which an interest was held by a person referred to

in any of paragraphs&#160;(a) to (d);</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>partnership in which an interest was held by a person

referred to in any of paragraphs&#160;(a) to (d).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the assumptions set out in subsection&#160;(5) are made:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the <sup>*</sup>member was a person referred to in any of

paragraphs&#160;(3)(a) to (d)&#151;the member; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the member was a trustee of a trust or a <sup>*</sup>partnership, being

a trust or partnership in which a person referred to in any of those paragraphs

held an interest&#151;the holder of the interest;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

would (if not an <sup>*</sup>Australian resident) be exempt from <sup>*</sup>withholding tax on the distribution or (if an Australian resident) be entitled to a <sup>*</sup>franking credit or a <sup>*</sup>tax offset in respect of the distribution.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The assumptions referred to in subsection&#160;(4) are that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the relevant former exempting entity was an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity

at the time it made the <sup>*</sup>distribution; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the distribution was a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution made to the

member; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the <sup>*</sup>member was a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity&#151;the

member was an exempting entity; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the member was a trustee of a trust or <sup>*</sup>partnership in which

a former exempting entity had an interest&#151;the former exempting entity was an

exempting entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person is taken to hold an interest in a trust, for the purposes of

paragraph&#160;(3)(e), if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is a beneficiary under the trust; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person derives, or will derive, income indirectly, through interposed

trusts or <sup>*</sup>partnerships, from <sup>*</sup>distributions received by

the trustee.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>A person is taken to hold an interest in a <sup>*</sup>partnership, for

the purposes of paragraph&#160;(3)(f), if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is a partner in the partnership; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person derives, or will derive, income indirectly, through interposed

trusts or partnerships, from <sup>*</sup>distributions received by the

partnership.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

208-160  Distributions that are affected by a manipulation of the imputation system

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		For the purposes of item&#160;2 of the table in section&#160;208-115 and

items&#160;2 and 5 of the table in section&#160;208-130, a

<sup>*</sup>distribution to an entity is affected by a manipulation of the

imputation system if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the Commissioner has made a determination under paragraph 204-30(3)(c)

that no <sup>*</sup>imputation benefit is to arise for the entity in respect of

the distribution; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Commissioner has made a determination under paragraph 177EA(5)(b) of

the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ that no franking credit benefit

(within the meaning of that section) is to arise in respect of the distribution

to the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the distribution is part of a <sup>*</sup>dividend stripping operation.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

208-165  Amount of the exempting credit or franking credit arising because of a distribution franked with an exempting credit

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Use the following formula to work out:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount of an <sup>*</sup>exempting credit arising under item&#160;2 of

the table in section&#160;208-115 because a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity

receives a <sup>*</sup>distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with an exempting

credit; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount of a <sup>*</sup>franking credit arising under item&#160;2 or 5

of the table in section&#160;208-130 because an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity

receives a distribution franked with an exempting credit;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1209.gif)</sub>

208-170  Where a determination under paragraph 177EA(5)(b) of the Income Tax Assessment Act 1936 affects part of the distribution

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Use the following formula to work out:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount of an <sup>*</sup>exempting credit arising under item&#160;3 of

the table in section&#160;208-115 because a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity

receives a <sup>*</sup>distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with an exempting

credit; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount of a <sup>*</sup>franking credit arising under item&#160;3 or 6

of the table in section&#160;208-130 because an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity

receives a distribution franked with an exempting credit;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

 <sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1210.gif)</sub>

208-175  When does a distribution franked with an exempting credit flow indirectly to an entity?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with an exempting credit is

taken to _flow indirectly_ to an entity if, had it been a

<sup>*</sup>franked distribution, it would have been taken to have flowed

indirectly to the entity under section&#160;207-35.

 </dl></dl>

208-180  What is an entity's share of the exempting credit on a distribution?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		To work out an entity's _share_ of the <sup>*</sup>exempting

credit on a <sup>*</sup>distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with that credit, use

section&#160;207-55 to work out what the entity's share of the credit would be

it if were a <sup>*</sup>franking credit on a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution.

The entity's share of the exempting credit is equal to that amount.

 </dl></dl>

208-185  Minister may convert exempting surplus to franking credit of former exempting entity previously owned by the Commonwealth

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Minister may make a determination or determinations under this section

if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at a particular time, a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity is an

<sup>*</sup>exempting entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at that time all of the <sup>*</sup>membership interests in the entity are

owned by the Commonwealth; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the Commonwealth has offered for sale or sold, or proposes to offer for

sale, some or all of the membership interests; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the Minister is satisfied, having regard to the matters mentioned in

subsection&#160;(2), that it is desirable to make a determination or

determinations under this section in relation to the entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The matters to which the Minister must have regard under

paragraph&#160;(1)(d) are:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>whether the making of the determination or determinations is necessary to

enable the entity to make <sup>*</sup>distributions <sup>*</sup>franked at a

<sup>*</sup>franking percentage of 100% after the sale; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the extent to which the success of the sale or proposed sale depended or

will depend upon the ability of the entity to make <sup>*</sup>franked

distributions; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the extent to which the reduction in receipts of income tax resulting from

the making of the determination or determinations would be offset by the

receipt of increased proceeds from the sale; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>any other matters that the Minister thinks relevant.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The following provisions of this section apply after the

<sup>*</sup>exempting entity becomes a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity would, apart from this section, have an <sup>*</sup>exempting surplus at the end of an income year, the Minister may, in writing, determine that: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>exempting debit of the entity (not exceeding the exempting

surplus) specified in the determination is taken to have arisen immediately

before the end of that income year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>franking credit of the entity equal to the amount of the

exempting debit is taken to have arisen immediately before the end of that

income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A determination under this section may be expressed to be subject to

compliance by the <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity with such conditions as

are specified in the determination.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>If a condition specified in a determination is not complied with, the Minister may revoke the determination and, if the Minister thinks it appropriate, make a further determination under subsection&#160;(4).</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>A determination, unless it is revoked, has effect according to its terms. </dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;208-G&#151;Tax effects of distributions by exempting entities
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;208-G
 208-190  What this Subdivision is about

Generally, a franked distribution from an exempting entity will only generate a tax effect for the recipient under Division&#160;207 if the recipient is also an exempting entity.
 A concession is made to employees of the entity who receive a franked distribution because they hold shares under an eligible employee share scheme.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

208-195	Division&#160;207 does not generally apply
 208-200	Distributions to exempting entities
 208-205	Distributions to employees acquiring shares under an eligible employee share scheme
 208-210	Subsidiaries
 208-215	Eligible employee share scheme

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 208-195  Division&#160;207 does not generally apply

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Division&#160;207 does not apply to a <sup>*</sup>distribution by an

<sup>*</sup>exempting entity, unless expressly applied under this Subdivision.

 </dl></dl>

208-200  Distributions to exempting entities

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Division&#160;207 applies to a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution made by an

<sup>*</sup>exempting entity to another exempting entity if the distribution

gives rise to a <sup>*</sup>franking credit for the other exempting entity

under item&#160;5 or 6 of the table in section&#160;208-130.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Division&#160;207 applies to a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution that is made by an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity and <sup>*</sup>flows indirectly to another exempting entity if the distribution gives rise to a <sup>*</sup>franking credit for that other entity under item&#160;7 of the table in section&#160;208-130\. </dd> </dl></dl>

208-205  Distributions to employees acquiring shares under an eligible employee share scheme

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Division&#160;207 also applies to a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution made by

an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the distribution is made to a person who is an employee of the exempting

entity, or of a <sup>*</sup>company that is a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary of the

exempting entity, at the time the distribution is made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the recipient acquired the <sup>*</sup>share on which the distribution is

made under an <sup>*</sup>employee share scheme in circumstances specified as

relevant in section&#160;208-215; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the recipient does not hold that share as a trustee.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

208-210  Subsidiaries

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The question whether a company  is a _subsidiary_ of

another company  is to be determined in the same way as the question

whether a corporation is a subsidiary of another corporation is determined

under the _Corporations Act 2001_.

 </dl></dl>

208-215  Eligible employee share scheme

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>share in a <sup>*</sup>company is acquired by a person under an

<sup>*</sup>employee share scheme in circumstances that are relevant for the

purposes of paragraph 208-205(b) and 208-235(b) if:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the share is acquired by the person in respect of, or for or in relation

directly or indirectly to, any employment of the person by the entity or by an

entity that is a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary of the company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>all the shares available for acquisition under the scheme are ordinary

shares or are preference shares to which are attached substantially the same

rights as are attached to ordinary shares; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>immediately after the acquisition of the shares:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the person does not hold a legal or beneficial interest in more than 5% of

the shares in the company; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the person is not in a position to control, or control the casting of,

more than 5% of the maximum number of votes that might be cast at a general

meeting of the company; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the share is not a <sup>*</sup>non-equity share.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;208-H&#151;Tax effect of a distribution franked with an exempting credit
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;208-H
 208-220  What this Subdivision is about

Generally, a distribution franked with an exempting credit will only generate a tax effect for the recipient under Division&#160;207 if a tax effect would have been generated for the recipient had the recipient received a franked distribution when the distributing entity was an exempting entity.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

208-225	Division&#160;207 does not generally apply
 208-230	Distributions to exempting entities and former exempting entities
 208-235	Distributions to employees acquiring shares under an eligible employee share scheme
 208-240	Distributions to certain individuals

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 208-225  Division&#160;207 does not generally apply

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Division&#160;207 does not apply to a <sup>*</sup>distribution

<sup>*</sup>franked with an exempting credit, unless the Division is expressly

applied to the distribution under this Subdivision.

 </dl></dl>

208-230  Distributions to exempting entities and former exempting entities

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Division&#160;207 applies to a <sup>*</sup>distribution <sup>*</sup>franked

with an exempting credit by a <sup>*</sup>former exempting entity as if it were

a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the recipient of the distribution is a former exempting entity and the

distribution gives rise to an <sup>*</sup>exempting credit for the recipient;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the recipient of the distribution is an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity and

the distribution gives rise to a <sup>*</sup>franking credit for the recipient;

or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the distribution <sup>*</sup>flows indirectly to a former exempting entity

and gives rise to an exempting credit for that entity; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the distribution flows indirectly to an exempting entity and gives rise to

a franking credit for that entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

208-235  Distributions to employees acquiring shares under an eligible employee share scheme

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Division&#160;207 also applies to a <sup>*</sup>distribution

<sup>*</sup>franked with an exempting credit made by a <sup>*</sup>former

exempting entity as if it were a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the distribution is made to a person who is an employee of the former

exempting entity, or of a <sup>*</sup>company that is a <sup>*</sup>subsidiary

of the former exempting entity, at the time the distribution is made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the recipient acquired the <sup>*</sup>share on which the distribution is

made under an <sup>*</sup>employee share scheme in circumstances specified as

relevant in section&#160;208-215; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the recipient does not hold that share as a trustee.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

208-240  Distributions to certain individuals

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Division&#160;207 also applies to a <sup>*</sup>distribution

<sup>*</sup>franked with an exempting credit made by a <sup>*</sup>former

exempting entity as if it were a <sup>*</sup>franked distribution if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>corporate tax entity other than a former exempting entity

became an <sup>*</sup>exempting entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>immediately before the entity became an exempting entity all the

accountable membership interests and accountable partial interests were

beneficially owned (whether directly or indirectly) by natural persons who were

<sup>*</sup>Australian residents; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity became an exempting entity because some or all of the persons

mentioned in paragraph&#160;(b) ceased to be Australian residents; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity becomes a former exempting entity because all of the persons

mentioned in paragraph&#160;(b) are or have become Australian residents; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>an amount attributable to a distribution <sup>*</sup>franked with an

exempting credit made by the entity is included in the assessable income of

such a person; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>all the accountable membership interests or accountable partial interests

in the entity were, throughout the period beginning when the entity became an

exempting entity and ending when the amount was received by the person,

beneficially owned (directly or indirectly) by the person mentioned in

paragraph&#160;(b); and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>the person is an eligible continuing substantial member in relation to the

distribution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

 </dl></dl>

or <sup>*</sup>public trading trust&#151;it is a unit in the trust.

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION, VALUE SHIFTING, DEMERGERS AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2002Schedule&#160;14&#151;Loss integrity rules: global method of valuing assets 
**</center>

<part>Part&#160;1&#151;Income Tax Assessment Act 1997</part>

1  Section&#160;165-115

Repeal the section, substitute:

165-115  What this Subdivision is about

If a change occurs in the ownership or control of a company that has an unrealised net loss, the company cannot, to the extent of the unrealised net loss, have capital losses taken into account, or deduct revenue losses, in respect of CGT events that happen to CGT assets that it owned at the time of the change, unless it satisfies the same business test.

165-115AA  Special rules to save compliance costs

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A company is exempt from these rules if, at the time of the change in

ownership or control, it (together with certain related entities) has a net

asset value of not more than $5,000,000 under the test in section&#160;152-15

(for small business CGT relief).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>In working out whether it has an unrealised net loss, a company can choose to work out the market value of each of its assets individually, or of all of its assets together.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a company works out the market value of each of its assets individually, it may choose to exclude every asset that it acquired for less than $10,000, in which case: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>unrealised losses and gains on the excluded assets will not be taken into

account in calculating the company's unrealised net loss; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>losses on the excluded assets will be allowed without the company being

subject to the same business test.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

2  At the end of subsection 165-115A(1B)

<center>Back to Top</center>

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		However, the choice does not affect the application of the <sup>*</sup>global

method of working out whether the company has an unrealised net loss (see

subsection 165-115E(2)).

 </dl></dl>

3  Section&#160;165-115E

After "this way", insert "(the _individual asset method_), unless the company chooses to work it out using the <sup>*</sup>global method (set out in subsection&#160;(2))".

4  At the end of section&#160;165-115E

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The _global method_ of working out whether the company has an

_unrealised net loss_ at the relevant time is as follows:

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Method statement_

_Step 1_.	Work out the total market value of all <sup>*</sup>CGT assets that the company owned at the relevant time (including those it <sup>*</sup>acquired for less than $10,000), using a valuation method that would generally be regarded as appropriate in the circumstances.
 _Step 2_.	Work out the total of the <sup>*</sup>cost bases of those <sup>*</sup>CGT assets at the relevant time.

	Note:	If a CGT asset that the company owned at the relevant time was also trading stock or a revenue asset at that time, see subsection&#160;(3) of this section.

_Step 3_.	If the step 2 amount exceeds the step 1 amount, the excess is the company's _preliminary unrealised net loss_ at the relevant time.
 _Step 4_.	Add up the company's preliminary unrealised net loss and any <sup>*</sup>capital loss, deduction or share of a deduction disregarded under section&#160;170-270 in relation to an asset referred to in paragraph 165-115A(1A)(b). The total is the company's _unrealised net loss_ at the relevant time.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset that the company owned at the relevant time was

also <sup>*</sup>trading stock or a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset at that time;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the asset's <sup>*</sup>cost base at the relevant time is _less than_

the amount that would be compared under section&#160;165-115F with the asset's

market value in working out a notional revenue gain or notional revenue loss

that the company has at the relevant time in respect of the asset;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then, for the purposes of step 2 of the method statement in subsection&#160;(2) of this section, the amount that would be so compared is to be taken into account _instead of_ that cost base.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A choice to use the <sup>*</sup>global method must be made on or before:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the day on which the company lodges its income tax return for the income

year in which the relevant time occurred; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>such later day as the Commissioner allows.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

5  Subsection 165-115F(7)

Repeal the subsection.

6  Section&#160;165-115G

Repeal the section, substitute:

165-115GA  What this Subdivision is about

This Subdivision prevents multiple recognition of a company's losses when significant equity and debt interests that entities (not individuals) have in the company are realised.

165-115GB  When adjustments must be made

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The operation of this Subdivision is triggered at an alteration time,

which is when:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an alteration takes place in the ownership or control of the company; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the liquidator of the company declares that shares in the company are

worthless (CGT event G3).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An alteration time is the trigger for making reductions and other

adjustments to the reduced cost base of significant equity and debt interests

in the company that are owned by an entity (not an individual) that, alone or

with its associates, has a controlling stake in the company and either:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>has a direct or indirect equity interest of at least 10% in the company;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is owed a debt of at least $10,000 by the company or by another entity

that has a significant equity or debt interest in the company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Deductions that relate to such interests held as trading stock or otherwise on revenue account are also reduced.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Adjustments may also be made when such an entity's interests in the

company are partly realised within 12 months before an alteration time or if,

under an arrangement, such interests are realised partly within that period or

at the alteration time and partly at an earlier time.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, entities in which there are no interests in respect of which the company's losses have been, or can be, duplicated are not affected by this Subdivision. </dd> </dl></dl>

165-115GC  How adjustments are calculated

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Adjustments are based on the overall loss of the company. This comprises

its realised losses and unrealised losses on CGT assets.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Special rules, directed at saving compliance costs, apply to determine whether unrealised losses have to be counted at an alteration time and, if so, how to work them out.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The company may not have to calculate its unrealised losses if the alteration time is not also a changeover time for the purposes of Subdivision&#160;165-CC (about change of ownership or control of a company that has an unrealised net loss), and the company has no realised losses.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The company does not have to count unrealised losses at an alteration time if (together with certain related entities) it has a net asset value of not more than $5,000,000 under the test in section&#160;152-15 (for small business CGT relief).</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>In working out its unrealised losses on CGT assets, the company can choose to work out the market value of each of its assets individually, or of all of its assets together.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the company works out the market value of each of its assets individually, unrealised losses on assets acquired for less than $10,000 do not have to be calculated at any time.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>Amounts (whether realised or unrealised) counted at a previous alteration time are not counted again at a later alteration time. (This does not apply to unrealised losses worked out by reference to the market value of all the company's assets together.)</dd> <dt>(8)</dt><dd>However, if unrealised amounts are _not_ counted at a previous alteration time (for example, because of the $10,000 or small business entity exclusions) and are not required to be taken into account in adjustments made at that time, they may be counted at a later time as part of a realised loss.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>A formula is provided for making adjustments in straightforward cases if applying the formula gives a reasonable result having regard to the object of the Subdivision. Otherwise, reasonable adjustments must be made having regard to a number of stated factors.</dd> <dt>(10)</dt><dd>To help entities to make the adjustments, any entity that, in its own right, has a controlling stake in the company is required to provide a written notice to its associates setting out relevant information. In limited circumstances, the company itself may have to provide a written notice to entities that, to its knowledge, have a significant equity or debt interest in it. </dd> </dl></dl>

Insert:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

if the company has chosen to use the <sup>*</sup>global method of working out

whether it has an adjusted unrealised loss at the alteration time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

if the company has chosen to use the <sup>*</sup>global method of working out

whether it has an adjusted unrealised loss at the current alteration time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>
