10  Subsection 165-115U(1)

After "this way", insert "(the _individual asset method_), unless the company chooses to work it out using the <sup>*</sup>global method (set out in subsection&#160;(1B))".

11  After subsection 165-115U(1)

Insert:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1A)</dt><dd>Step 1 in the method statement in subsection&#160;(1) does not apply to

an amount that was counted at an earlier alteration time if the company has

chosen to use the <sup>*</sup>global method of working out whether it has an

adjusted unrealised loss at that earlier time.</dd> <dt>(1B)</dt><dd>The _global method_ of working out whether the company has an _adjusted unrealised loss_ at the relevant alteration time is as follows: </dd> </dl></dl>

_Method statement_

_Step 1_.	Work out the total market value of all <sup>*</sup>CGT assets that the company owned at the relevant alteration time (including those it <sup>*</sup>acquired for less than $10,000), using a valuation method that would generally be regarded as appropriate in the circumstances.
 _Step 2_.	Work out the total of the <sup>*</sup>cost bases of those <sup>*</sup>CGT assets at the relevant time.

	Note:	If a CGT asset that the company owned at the relevant time was also trading stock or a revenue asset at that time, see subsection&#160;(1C) of this section.

_Step 3_.	If the step 2 amount exceeds the step 1 amount, the excess is the company's _adjusted unrealised loss_ at the relevant time.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1C)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset that the company owned at the relevant alteration

time was also <sup>*</sup>trading stock or a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset at that

time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the asset's <sup>*</sup>cost base at the relevant alteration time is

_less than_ the amount that, if the relevant alteration time were a

changeover time, would be compared under section&#160;165-115F with the asset's

market value in working out a notional revenue gain or notional revenue loss

that the company would have at the changeover time in respect of the asset;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then, for the purposes of step 2 of the method statement in subsection&#160;(1B) of this section, the amount that would be so compared is to be taken into account _instead of_ that cost base.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1D)</dt><dd>A choice to use the <sup>*</sup>global method must be made on or before:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the day on which the company lodges its income tax return for the income

year in which the relevant alteration time occurred; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>such later day as the Commissioner allows.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

12  Subsection 165-115V(8)

Repeal the subsection.

13  After subsection 165-115W(1)

Insert:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1A)</dt><dd>Step 2 in the method statement in subsection&#160;(1) does not apply to

an amount counted at an earlier alteration time if the company has chosen to

use the <sup>*</sup>global method of working out whether it has an adjusted

unrealised loss at that earlier time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

14  At the end of subsection 165-115ZA(1)

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This section and section&#160;165-115ZB can apply

differently for a company that has used the global method of working out

whether it has an adjusted unrealised loss at an alteration time. See

section&#160;165-115ZD.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

15  At the end of Subdivision&#160;165-CD

Add:

165-115ZD  Adjustment (or further adjustment) for interest realised at a loss after global method has been used

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section affects how sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB apply to an

interest (the _equity_) in, or a debt owed by, a company if, apart

from this section, a loss:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>would be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to the equity or debt; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>would be so realised but for Subdivision&#160;170-D (which defers

realisation of capital losses and deductions);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

and the company chose to use the <sup>*</sup>global method of working out whether it had an adjusted unrealised loss at the last alteration time:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that happened for the company before the realisation event; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>immediately before which the equity or debt was, or was part of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the company was a <sup>*</sup>loss company at that alteration time&#151;a

relevant equity interest, or a relevant debt interest, that an entity had in

the company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;what would have been such an interest if the company had been

a loss company at that alteration time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If that last alteration time is before the day on which the

_New Business Tax System (Consolidation, Value Shifting, Demergers and Other Measures) Act 2002_ received the Royal Assent, the owner of the equity or

debt may choose to apply section&#160;165-115ZD of the _Income Tax (Transitional Provisions) Act 1997_ instead of this section.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In addition to any application to the equity or debt, in relation to that

last alteration time, that sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB have apart

from this section, those sections apply (and are taken always to have applied)

to the equity or debt, in relation to that last alteration time, as if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company had an adjusted unrealised loss at that time worked out under

this section; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company were therefore a <sup>*</sup>loss company at that time; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that adjusted unrealised loss were the company's overall loss at that time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of how sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB apply

because of this section, the adjustment amount under section&#160;165-115ZB is

to be worked out and applied in accordance with subsection 165-115ZB(6) (the

non-formula method).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Adjusted unrealised loss worked out under this section_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The adjusted unrealised loss referred to in paragraph&#160;(2)(a) is

worked out using this method statement:

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Method statement_

_Step 1._	Add up the amount or value of each thing covered by subsection&#160;(5).
 _Step 2._	If the step 1 amount exceeds the loss referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a), reduce the step 1 amount by the excess.
 _Step 3._	Reduce the step 2 amount by so much of the loss referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a) as it is reasonable to conclude is attributable to _none_ of these:

	(a)	a notional capital loss, or a notional revenue loss, that the company has at that last alteration time in respect of a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset;
 	(b)	a trading stock decrease in relation to that time for a CGT asset that was <sup>*</sup>trading stock of the company at that time.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>This subsection covers each thing covered by an item in the table, except

to the extent that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>it is reasonable to conclude that the thing was _not_ attributable to

value that is reflected in a notional capital gain or notional revenue gain

that the company has at that last alteration time in respect of a

<sup>*</sup>CGT asset; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the thing has resulted in a reduction of the <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base

of the equity or debt.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

 </dl></dl>

if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A notice under subsection 165-115ZC(4) or (5) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ must be given within 6 months after the day on which

the _New Business Tax System (Consolidation, Value Shifting, Demergers and Other Measures) Act 2002_ received the Royal Assent if the alteration time

is before that day.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If, because of amendments made by Schedule&#160;14 to the _New Business Tax System (Consolidation, Value Shifting, Demergers and Other Measures) Act 2002_, a notice already given under subsection 165-115ZC(4) or (5) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ before the day referred to in subsection&#160;(1) of this section no longer complies with section&#160;165-115ZC of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_, the entity required to give the notice may comply with that section&#160;165-115ZC by giving a further notice.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The further notice: </dd> </dl></dl>

(which may include setting out additional information) that the notice as

varied complies with section&#160;165-115ZC of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ as affected by the amendments; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>must be given within the 6 months referred to in subsection&#160;(1) of

this section, or within a further period allowed by the Commissioner; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>must otherwise be given in accordance with that section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

165-115ZD  Adjustment (or further adjustment) for interest realised at a loss after global method has been used

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section affects how sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ apply to an interest (the

_equity_) in, or a debt owed by, a company if apart from this

section, a loss:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>would be realised for income tax purposes by a realisation event that

happens to the equity or debt; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>would be so realised but for Subdivision&#160;170-D of that Act (which

defers realisation of capital losses and deductions);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

and the company chose to use the global method of working out whether it had an adjusted unrealised loss at the last alteration time:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that happened for the company, before the realisation event; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>immediately before which the equity or debt was, or was part of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the company was a loss company at that alteration time&#151;a relevant

equity interest, or a relevant debt interest, that an entity had in the

company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;what would have been such an interest if the company had been

a loss company at that alteration time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

and these conditions are satisfied:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>that last alteration time is before the day on which the _New Business Tax System (Consolidation, Value Shifting, Demergers and Other Measures) Act 2002_ received the Royal Assent; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the entity that owns the equity or debt immediately before the realisation

event chooses to apply this section to the equity or debt, in relation to that

last alteration time, instead of section&#160;165-115ZD of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_; and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>the choice is made on or before the latest of these:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the last day of the period of 6 months after the day referred to in

paragraph&#160;(c) of this subsection;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the day on which the entity lodges its income tax return for the income

year in which the realisation event occurred;</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>such later day as the Commissioner allows.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

If the entity makes that choice, this section applies accordingly instead of 
<center>Back to Top</center>
 that section.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In addition to any application to the equity or debt, in relation to that

last alteration time, that sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ have apart from this section, those

sections apply (and are taken always to have applied) to the equity or debt, in

relation to that last alteration time, as if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company had an adjusted unrealised loss at that time equal to the loss

referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a) of this section, except so much of the

loss as it is reasonable to conclude is attributable to _none_ of these:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a notional capital loss, or a notional revenue loss, that the company has

at that last alteration time in respect of a CGT asset;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a trading stock decrease in relation to that time for a CGT asset that

was trading stock of the company at that time; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company were therefore a <sup>*</sup>loss company at that time; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that adjusted unrealised loss were the company's overall loss at that time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of how sections&#160;165-115ZA and 165-115ZB of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ apply because of this section, the

adjustment amount under section&#160;165-115ZB of that Act is to be worked out

and applied in accordance with subsection 165-115ZB(6) (the non-formula method)

of that Act.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a notice need not be given under section&#160;165-115ZC of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ because of this section; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>this section does not affect the requirements that apply to a notice that

otherwise must be given under that section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part&#160;3&#151;Dictionary amendments 

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

17  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_global method_:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>of working out whether a company has an unrealised net loss at a

particular time, has the meaning given by section&#160;165-115E; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of working out whether a company has an adjusted unrealised loss at a

particular time, has the meaning given by section&#160;165-115U.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

18  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_individual asset method_:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>of working out whether a company has an unrealised net loss at a

particular time, has the meaning given by section&#160;165-115E; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of working out whether a company has an adjusted unrealised loss at a

particular time, has the meaning given by section&#160;165-115U.

</dd>

Part&#160;4&#151;Application of amendments
 19  Application

The amendments made by this Schedule apply to a time at or after 1 pm (by legal time in the Australian Capital Territory) on 11&#160;November 1999.

<center>Back to Top</center>

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION, VALUE SHIFTING, DEMERGERS AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2002Schedule&#160;15&#151;Value shifting 
**</center>

 Part&#160;1&#151;New Divisions inserted in the Income Tax Assessment Act 1997
 1  After Part&#160;3-90

Insert: 

<part>Part&#160;3-95&#151;Value shifting</part>

Division&#160;723&#151;Direct value shifting by creating right over non-depreciating asset

Table of Subdivisions

723-A	Reduction in loss from realising non-depreciating asset
 723-B	Reducing reduced cost base of interests in entity that acquires non-depreciating asset under roll-over

Subdivision&#160;723-A&#151;Reduction in loss from realising non-depreciating asset

Table of sections

723-1	Object
 723-10	Reduction in loss from realising non-depreciating asset over which right has been created
 723-15	Reduction in loss from realising non-depreciating asset at the same time as right is created over it
 723-20	Exceptions
 723-25	Realisation event that is only a partial realisation
 723-35	Multiple rights created to take advantage of the $50,000 threshold
 723-40	Application to CGT asset that is also trading stock or revenue asset
 723-50	Effects if right created over underlying asset is also trading stock or a revenue asset

723-1  Object

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The purpose of this Division is to reduce a loss that would otherwise be

<sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a <sup>*</sup>realisation event

happening to an asset (except a <sup>*</sup>depreciating asset), to the extent

that:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>value has been shifted out of the asset by the owner creating in an

associate a right over the asset; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the value shifted was not brought to tax when the right was created and

has not since been brought to tax on a realisation of the right.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

723-10  Reduction in loss from realising non-depreciating asset over which right has been created

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A loss that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income

tax purposes by a <sup>*</sup>realisation event is reduced by the amount worked

out under subsections&#160;(3) and (4) if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the event happens to a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset (the _underlying asset_) you own that, at the time of the event (the _realisation time_):

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is _not_ a <sup>*</sup>depreciating asset; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is an item of your <sup>*</sup>trading stock; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>is a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset of yours; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>before the realisation time:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>you created in an <sup>*</sup>associate of yours; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an entity covered by subsection&#160;(2) (about previous owners of the

underlying asset) created in an associate of the entity;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		a right in respect of the underlying asset; and

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>immediately before the realisation time, the right is still in existence

and is owned by an associate of yours; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a decrease in the underlying asset's market value is reasonably

attributable to the creating of the right; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>creating the right involved a <sup>*</sup>CGT event:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>whose <sup>*</sup>capital proceeds are _less_ than the market value

of the right when created (the difference between those capital proceeds and

that market value is called the _shortfall on creating the right_);

and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>that is _not_ a CGT event that happens to some part of the

underlying asset but not to the remainder of it; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the shortfall on creating the right is more than $50,000; and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>the market value of the underlying asset at the realisation time is less

than it would have been if the right no longer existed at that time (the

difference is called the _deficit on realisation_).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If subparagraph&#160;(1)(e)(ii) applies, the cost base and

reduced cost base of the underlying asset is apportioned under

section&#160;112-30, so there is no need for this section to apply to the right.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This subsection covers an entity if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity <sup>*</sup>acquired the underlying asset before you did; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>there has been a roll-over for each <sup>*</sup>CGT event (if any) as a

result of which an entity (including you) acquired the asset after the first

entity acquired it, and before the realisation time; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>for each such CGT event (if any), the entity (including you) that acquired

the underlying asset as a result of the event was, immediately after the event,

an <sup>*</sup>associate of the entity that last acquired the asset before the

event.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The amount by which this section reduces the loss is the lesser of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the shortfall on creating the right; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the deficit on realisation.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

However, that amount is reduced by each gain that:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>is <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to the right:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>before or at the realisation time for the underlying asset; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>at a time when the right is owned by an entity that is your

<sup>*</sup>associate immediately before the realisation time for the

underlying asset; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>is not disregarded.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	To work out a gain realised for income tax purposes by a

realisation event that happens to the right, see sections&#160;977-15, 977-35,

977-40 and 977-55\. If more than one of those sections applies to the right, see

section&#160;723-50.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For each gain that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to the right:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>within 4 years after the realisation time for the underlying asset; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>at a time when the right is owned by an entity that is your

<sup>*</sup>associate immediately before the realisation time for the

underlying asset; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is not disregarded;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the amount worked out under subsection&#160;(3) is taken to have been reduced by the amount of that gain.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This subsection may result in amendment of an assessment

for the income year in which the realisation time happens.

 </dl></dl>

723-15  Reduction in loss from realising non-depreciating asset at the same time as right is created over it

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A loss that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for

income tax purposes by a <sup>*</sup>realisation event is reduced by the amount

worked out under subsections&#160;(2) and (3) if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the event happens to a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset (the _underlying asset_) you own that, at the time of the event (the _realisation time_):

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is _not_ a <sup>*</sup>depreciating asset; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is an item of your <sup>*</sup>trading stock;</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>is a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset of yours; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at the realisation time, you create in an <sup>*</sup>associate of yours a

right in respect of the underlying asset; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>creating the right involves a <sup>*</sup>CGT event:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>whose <sup>*</sup>capital proceeds are _less_ than the market value

of the right when created (the difference between those capital proceeds and

that market value is called the _shortfall on creating the right_);

and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>that is _not_ a CGT event that happens to some part of the

underlying asset but not to the remainder of it; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the shortfall on creating the right is more than $50,000; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the market value of the underlying asset at the realisation time is less

than it would have been if the right had not been created (the difference is

called the _deficit on realisation_).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If subparagraph&#160;(1)(c)(ii) applies, the cost base and

reduced cost base of the underlying asset is apportioned under

section&#160;112-30, so there is no need for this section to apply to the right.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The amount by which this section reduces the loss is the lesser of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the shortfall on creating the right; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the deficit on realisation.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For each gain that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to the right:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>within 4 years after the realisation time for the underlying asset; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>at a time when the right is owned by an entity that is your

<sup>*</sup>associate immediately before the realisation time for the

underlying asset; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is not disregarded;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the amount worked out under subsection&#160;(2) is taken to have been reduced by the amount of that gain.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	To work out a gain realised for income tax purposes by a

realisation event that happens to the right, see sections&#160;977-15, 977-35,

977-40 and 977-55\. If more than one of those sections applies to the right, see

section&#160;723-50\. Note 2:	This subsection may require amendment of an assessment for the income year in which the realisation time happens.  </dl></dl>

723-20  Exceptions

_Conservation covenant over land_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Section&#160;723-10 or 723-15 does not reduce a loss if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the underlying asset is land; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the right referred to in paragraph 723-10(1)(b) or 723-15(1)(b) is a

<sup>*</sup>conservation covenant over the land.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Right created on death of owner_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Section&#160;723-10 or 723-15 does not reduce a loss if the right referred

to in paragraph 723-10(1)(b) or 723-15(1)(b) is created by:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a will or codicil; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an order of a court varying or modifying a will or codicil; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a total or partial intestacy; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an order of a court varying or modifying the application of the law about

distributing the estate of someone who dies intestate.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

723-25  Realisation event that is only a partial realisation

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Section&#160;723-10 or 723-15 applies differently if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>realisation event happens to some part of a <sup>*</sup>CGT

asset (the _underlying asset_) you own that, at the time of the

event:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is _not_ a <sup>*</sup>depreciating asset; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is an item of your <sup>*</sup>trading stock; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>is a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset of yours;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		but not to the remainder of the underlying asset; or

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a realisation event consists of creating an interest in a CGT asset (also

the _underlying asset_) you own that, at the time of the event, is

covered by subparagraph&#160;(a)(i), (ii) or (iii).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The section applies on the basis that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>realisation event happens to the underlying asset; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the shortfall on creating the right referred to in paragraph 723-10(1)(e)

or 723-15(1)(c); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the deficit on realisation referred to in paragraph 723-10(1)(g) or

723-15(1)(e);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

are each reduced by multiplying its amount by this fraction:

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1211.gif)</sub>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of the formula in subsection&#160;(2):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_market value of part_ means the market value, at the time of the

<sup>*</sup>realisation event, of the part referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a)

or the interest referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(b), as appropriate. _market value of underlying asset_ means the market value, immediately before the <sup>*</sup>realisation event, of the underlying asset.  </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 723-35.]_

723-35  Multiple rights created to take advantage of the $50,000 threshold

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Sections&#160;723-10 and 723-15 apply differently if, having regard to all

relevant circumstances, it is reasonable to conclude that the sole or main

reason why a right was created as a different right from one or more other

rights created in respect of the same thing was so that paragraph 723-10(1)(f)

or 723-15(1)(d) would not be satisfied for one or more of the rights mentioned

in this subsection.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Those sections: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>apply to that thing, in relation to each of the rights mentioned in

subsection&#160;(1) of this section, as if paragraphs 723-10(1)(f) and

723-15(1)(d) were omitted; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>are taken always to have so applied.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

723-40  Application to CGT asset that is also trading stock or revenue asset

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset you own is also an item of your

<sup>*</sup>trading stock or a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset, this Division applies

to the asset once in its character as a CGT asset and again in its character as

trading stock or a revenue asset.

 </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 723-50.]_

723-50  Effects if right created over underlying asset is also trading stock or a revenue asset

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subsection 723-10(3) or (4) or 723-15(3) applies differently if the right

created in respect of the underlying asset is also <sup>*</sup>trading stock or

a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset at the time of a <sup>*</sup>realisation event that

happens to the right.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The gain that is taken into account for the purposes of that subsection is: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the right is also trading stock&#151;worked out under section&#160;977-35

or 977-40 (about realisation events for trading stock); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the right is also a revenue asset&#151;the greater of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the gain worked out under section&#160;977-15 (about realisation events

for CGT assets); and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the gain worked out under section&#160;977-55 (about realisation events

for revenue assets).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;723-B&#151;Reducing reduced cost base of interests in entity that acquires non-depreciating asset under roll-over

Table of sections

723-105	Reduced cost base of interest reduced when interest realised at a loss
 723-110	Direct and indirect roll-over replacement for underlying asset

723-105  Reduced cost base of interest reduced when interest realised at a loss

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of a <sup>*</sup>primary equity

interest, <sup>*</sup>secondary equity interest, or <sup>*</sup>indirect

primary equity interest, in a company or trust is reduced just before a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that is a <sup>*</sup>CGT event happens to the

interest if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>apart from this Division, a loss would be <sup>*</sup>realised for income

tax purposes by the CGT event; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>apart from this Division, a loss would have been <sup>*</sup>realised for

income tax purposes by a realisation event if the event had happened, just

before the CGT event, to a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset (the _underlying asset_) that the company or trust then owned and that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>was _not_ then a <sup>*</sup>depreciating asset; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>was then an item of <sup>*</sup>trading stock of the company or trust;

or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>was then a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset of the company or trust; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the loss referred to in paragraph&#160;(b) would have been reduced under

Subdivision&#160;723-A by an amount (the _underlying asset loss reduction_); and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>for the entity (the _transferor_) that owned the interest just

before the CGT event, the interest was a <sup>*</sup>direct roll-over

replacement or <sup>*</sup>indirect roll-over replacement for the underlying

asset.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the interest was a <sup>*</sup>direct roll-over replacement, its

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost base is reduced by the amount worked out using this

formula, unless that amount does not appropriately reflect the matters referred

to in subsection&#160;(4):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1212.gif)</sub>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of the formula in subsection&#160;(2):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_RCB of interest_ means the interest's <sup>*</sup>reduced cost

base when the transferor <sup>*</sup>acquired it. _total of RCBs of direct roll-over replacements_ means the total of the <sup>*</sup>reduced cost bases of all <sup>*</sup>direct roll-over replacements for the underlying asset when the transferor <sup>*</sup>acquired them.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the interest was an <sup>*</sup>indirect roll-over replacement; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount worked out under subsection&#160;(2) does not appropriately

reflect the matters referred to in this subsection;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the interest's <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base is reduced by an amount that is appropriate having regard to these matters:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the underlying asset loss reduction; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the quantum of the interest relative to all <sup>*</sup>direct roll-over

replacements and indirect roll-over replacements that the transferor owns or

has previously owned.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

723-110  Direct and indirect roll-over replacement for underlying asset

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For an entity (the _transferor_) that owns a <sup>*</sup>CGT

asset, the CGT asset is a _direct roll-over replacement_ for

something (the _underlying asset_) that another entity owns if, and

only if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>CGT event happened to the underlying asset while the

transferor owned it; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the other entity <sup>*</sup>acquired the underlying asset as a result of

that CGT event; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>there was a <sup>*</sup>replacement-asset roll-over for the CGT event;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the transferor received the CGT asset (or CGT assets including it) in

respect of the CGT event as the replacement asset (or the replacement assets).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For an entity (the _transferor_) that owns a <sup>*</sup>CGT

asset, the CGT asset is an _indirect roll-over replacement_ for

something (the _underlying asset_) that another entity owns if, and

only if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>CGT event happened to another CGT asset at a time when the

transferor owned it and the other entity already owned the underlying asset;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for the transferor, the other CGT asset was at that time:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>direct roll-over replacement for the underlying asset; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an indirect roll-over replacement for the underlying asset because of any

other application or applications of this subsection; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>there was a <sup>*</sup>replacement-asset roll-over for the CGT event;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the transferor received the first CGT asset (or CGT assets including it)

in respect of the CGT event as the replacement asset (or the replacement assets).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Division&#160;725&#151;Direct value shifting affecting interests in companies and trusts

Table of Subdivisions

	Guide to Division&#160;725
 725-A	Scope of the direct value shifting rules
 725-B	What is a direct value shift
 725-C	Consequences of a direct value shift
 725-D	Consequences for down interest or up interest as CGT asset
 725-E	Consequences for down interest or up interest as trading stock or a revenue asset
 725-F	Value adjustments and taxed gains

Guide to Division&#160;725
 725-1  What this Division is about

If, under a scheme, value is shifted from equity or loan interests in a company or trust to other equity or loan interests in the same company or trust (including interests issued at a discount), this Division:

	(a)	adjusts the value of those interests for income tax purposes to take account of material changes in market value that are attributable to the value shift; and
 	(b)	treats the value shift as a partial realisation to the extent that value is shifted between interests held by different owners, and in some other cases.

However, it does so only for interests that are owned by entities involved in the value shift.

Subdivision&#160;725-A&#151;Scope of the direct value shifting rules 

Table of sections

725-45	Main object
 725-50	When a direct value shift has consequences under this Division
 725-55	Controlling entity test
 725-65	Cause of the value shift
 725-70	Consequences for down interest only if there is a material decrease in its market value
 725-80	Who is an affected owner of a down interest?
 725-85	Who is an affected owner of an up interest?
 725-90	Direct value shift that will be reversed
 725-95	Direct value shift resulting from reversal

725-45  Main object

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The main object of this Division is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to prevent inappropriate losses from arising on the realisation of

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests from which value has been shifted to other

equity or loan interests in the same entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to prevent inappropriate gains from arising on the realisation of equity

or loan interests in the same entity to which the value has been shifted;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

so far as those interests are owned by entities involved in the value shift.

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This is done by:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>adjusting the value of those interests for income tax purposes to take

account of changes in market value that are attributable to the value shift;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>treating the value shift as a partial realisation to the extent that value

is shifted:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>between interests held by different owners; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>in the case of interests in their character as CGT assets&#151;from post-CGT

assets to pre-CGT assets; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>between interests of different characters.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

725-50  When a direct value shift has consequences under this Division

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>direct value shift under a <sup>*</sup>scheme involving

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests in an entity (the _target entity_) has consequences for you under this Division if, and only if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the target entity is a company or trust at some time during the

<sup>*</sup>scheme period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;725-55 (Controlling entity test) is satisfied; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>section&#160;725-65 (Cause of the value shift) is satisfied; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>you are an <sup>*</sup>affected owner of a <sup>*</sup>down interest, or

an <sup>*</sup>affected owner of an <sup>*</sup>up interest, or both; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>neither of sections&#160;725-90 and 725-95 (about direct value shifts that

are reversed) applies.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For a down interest of which you are an affected owner, the

direct value shift has consequences under this Division only if

section&#160;725-70 (about material decrease in market value) is satisfied.

 </dl></dl>

725-55  Controlling entity test

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An entity (the _controller_) must <sup>*</sup>control (for value

shifting purposes) the target entity at some time during the period starting

when the <sup>*</sup>scheme is entered into and ending when it has been carried

out. (That period is the _scheme period_.)

 </dl></dl>

For the concept of _control (for value shifting purposes)_,
see sections&#160;727-355 to 727-375.

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 725-65.]_

725-65  Cause of the value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>It must be the case that one or more of the following:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the target entity;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the controller;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an entity that was an <sup>*</sup>associate of the controller at some time

during or after the <sup>*</sup>scheme period;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>active participant in the <sup>*</sup>scheme;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

(either alone or together with one or more other entities) did under the scheme the one or more things:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>to which the decrease in the market value of the <sup>*</sup>down

interests is reasonably attributable; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>to which the increase in the market value of the <sup>*</sup>up interests,

or the issue of up interests at a <sup>*</sup>discount, is reasonably

attributable, or that is or include the issue of up interests at a

<sup>*</sup>discount.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Active participants (if target entity is closely held)_

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An entity (the _first entity_) is an _active participant_ in the <sup>*</sup>scheme if, and only if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at some time during the <sup>*</sup>scheme period, the target entity has

fewer than 300 members (in the case of a company) or fewer than 300

beneficiaries (in the case of a trust); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first entity has actively participated in, or directly facilitated,

the entering into or carrying out of the <sup>*</sup>scheme (whether or not it

did so at the direction of some other entity); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the first entity:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>owns a <sup>*</sup>down interest at the <sup>*</sup>decrease time; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>owns an <sup>*</sup>up interest at the <sup>*</sup>increase time or has

an up interest issued to it at a <sup>*</sup>discount because of the

<sup>*</sup>direct value shift.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_When an entity has 300 or more members or beneficiaries_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Section&#160;124-810 (under which certain companies and trusts are not

regarded as having 300 or more members or beneficiaries) also applies for the

purposes of this Division.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>In addition, this Division applies to a <sup>*</sup>non-fixed trust as if it did not have 300 or more beneficiaries. </dd> </dl></dl>

725-70  Consequences for down interest only if there is a material decrease in its market value

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>For a <sup>*</sup>down interest of which you are an <sup>*</sup>affected

owner, the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift has consequences under this Division

only if the sum of the decreases in the market value of all down interests

because of direct value shifts under the same <sup>*</sup>scheme as the direct

value shift is at least $150,000.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	In working out the sum of the decreases in market value of

all down interests, it will be necessary to include decreases not only in your

down interests, but also in those of other affected owners and of entities that

are not affected owners.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, if, having regard to all relevant circumstances, it is reasonable

to conclude that the sole or main reason why a <sup>*</sup>direct value shift

happened under a different scheme from one or more other direct value shifts

was so that subsection&#160;(1) would not be satisfied for one or more of the

direct value shifts mentioned in this subsection, subsection&#160;(1) does not

apply (and is taken never to have applied) to any of the direct value shifts.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 725-80.]_

725-80  Who is an affected owner of a down interest?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An entity is an _affected owner_ of a <sup>*</sup>down interest

if, and only if, the entity owns the down interest at the <sup>*</sup>decrease

time and at least one of these paragraphs is satisfied:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity is the controller;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity was an <sup>*</sup>associate of the controller at some time

during or after the <sup>*</sup>scheme period;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity is an <sup>*</sup>active participant in the <sup>*</sup>scheme.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

725-85  Who is an affected owner of an up interest?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An entity is an _affected owner_ of an <sup>*</sup>up interest

if, and only if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>there is at least one <sup>*</sup>affected owner of <sup>*</sup>down

interests; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the entity owns the up interest at the <sup>*</sup>increase time, or the

interest is an up interest because it was issued to the entity at a

<sup>*</sup>discount;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

and at least one of these paragraphs is satisfied:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the entity is the controller;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the entity was an <sup>*</sup>associate of the controller at some time

during or after the <sup>*</sup>scheme period;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>at some time during or after the scheme period, the entity was an

associate of an entity that is an affected owner of down interests because it

was an associate of the controller at some time during or after that period;</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the entity is an <sup>*</sup>active participant in the <sup>*</sup>scheme.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

725-90  Direct value shift that will be reversed

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>direct value shift does _not_ have consequences for

you under this Division if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the one or more things referred to in paragraph 725-145(1)(b) brought

about a state of affairs, but for which the direct value shift would not have

happened; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>as at the time referred to in that paragraph, it is more likely than not

that, because of the <sup>*</sup>scheme, that state of affairs will cease to

exist within 4 years after that time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Example:	Under a scheme, the voting rights attached to a class of

shares in a company are changed. As a result, the market value of shares in

that class decreases, and the market value of other classes of shares in the

company increases. The company's constitution provides that the change is to

last for only 3 years.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, this section stops applying if the state of affairs referred to

in paragraph&#160;(1)(a) still exists:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at the end of those 4 years; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>when a <sup>*</sup>realisation event happens to <sup>*</sup>down interests

or <sup>*</sup>up interests of which you are, or any other entity is, an

<sup>*</sup>affected owner;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

whichever happens sooner.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If this section stops applying, it is taken _never_ to have applied

to the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This may result in an assessment for an earlier income year

having to be amended to give effect to the consequences that the direct value

shift would have had for you under this Division if this section hadn't applied.

 </dl></dl>

725-95  Direct value shift resulting from reversal

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A <sup>*</sup>direct value shift does not have consequences for any entity

under this Division if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;725-90 applies, and the state of affairs referred to in

paragraph 725-90(1)(a) ceases to exist; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the direct value shift would not have happened but for that state of

affairs ceasing to exist.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, if section&#160;725-90 stops applying, this section is taken

_never_ to have applied to the later direct value shift.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;725-B&#151;What is a direct value shift 

Table of sections 

<center>Back to Top</center>

725-145	When there is a _direct value shift_
 725-150	Issue of equity or loan interests at a _discount_
 725-155	Meaning of _down interests_, _decrease time_, _up interests_ and _increase time_
 725-160	What is the nature of a direct value shift?
 725-165	If market value decrease or increase is only partly attributable to the scheme

725-145  When there is a direct value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>There is a _direct value shift_ under a <sup>*</sup>scheme

involving <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests in an entity (the _target entity_) if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>there is a decrease in the market value of one or more equity or loan

interests in the target entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the decrease is reasonably attributable to one or more things done under

the scheme, and occurs at or after the time when that thing, or the first of

those things, is done; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>either or both of subsections&#160;(2) and (3) are satisfied.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Examples of something done under a scheme are issuing new shares at a <sup>*</sup>discount, buying back shares or changing the voting rights attached to shares.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>One or more <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests in the target entity must be

issued at a <sup>*</sup>discount. The issue must be, or must be reasonably

attributable to, the thing, or one or more of the things, referred to in

paragraph&#160;(1)(b). It must also occur at or after the time referred to in

that paragraph.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Example:	A company runs a family business. There are 2 shares

originally issued for $2 each. They are owned by husband and wife. The market

value of the shares is much greater (represented by the value of the assets of

the company less its liabilities). The company issues one more share for $2 to

their son. 	Caution is needed in such a situation. The example would result in a large CGT liability for the husband and wife under this Division, because they have shifted 1/3 of the value of their own shares to their son. No such liability would arise if the share had been issued for its market value.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Or, there must be an increase in the market value of one or more

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests in the target entity. The increase must be

reasonably attributable to the thing, or to one or more of the things, referred

to in paragraph&#160;(1)(b). It must also occur at or after the time referred

to in that paragraph.

</dd> </dl></dl>

725-150  Issue of equity or loan interests at a discount

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest is issued at a

_discount_ if, and only if, the market value of the interest when

issued exceeds the amount of the payment that the issuing entity receives. The

excess is the amount of the _discount_.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The payment that the issuing entity receives can include property. If it does, use the market value of the property in working out the amount of the payment. </dd> </dl></dl>

_Amounts for which bonus equities are treated as being issued_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>primary equity interest is issued as mentioned in subsection

130-20(1) (about bonus equities issued in relation to original equities); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>subsection 130-20(3) does _not_ apply (about bonus equities that are

a dividend or otherwise assessable income);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

subsection&#160;(1) of this section applies to the interest as if the amount 
<center>Back to Top</center>
 of the payment that the issuing entity receives were equal to the <sup>*</sup>cost base of the interest when issued (as worked out under section&#160;130-20).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>primary equity interest is issued as mentioned in subsection

6BA(1) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ (about bonus shares issued

in relation to original shares); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>subsection 6BA(2) of that Act applies (about bonus shares that are a

dividend);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

subsection&#160;(1) of this section applies to the interest as if the amount of the payment that the issuing entity receives were equal to the consideration worked out under subsection 6BA(2) of that Act.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If both of subsections&#160;(3) and (4) apply to the issue of the same

<sup>*</sup>primary equity interest, subsection&#160;(1) of this section

applies to the interest as if the amount of the payment that the issuing entity

receives were equal to the greater of the amounts worked out under

subsections&#160;(3) and (4).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Application of subsectionsÂ (3), (4) and (5)_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>Subsection&#160;(3) does not apply if, for the income year in which the

interest is issued, the issuing entity is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a corporate unit trust within the meaning of section&#160;102J of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a public trading trust within the meaning of section&#160;102R of that Act.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>Subsections&#160;(3), (4) and (5) have effect only for the purposes of

working out whether a <sup>*</sup>direct value shift has happened and, if so,

its consequences (if any) under this Division.

</dd> </dl></dl>

725-155  Meaning of down interests, decrease time, up interests and increase time

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in the target entity is a

_down interest_ if a decrease in its market value is reasonably

attributable to the one or more things referred to in paragraph 725-145(1)(b),

and occurs at or after the time referred to in that paragraph. The time when

the decrease happens is called the _decrease time_ for that

interest.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in the target entity is an _up interest_ if subsection 725-145(2) or (3) is satisfied for the interest. The time when the interest is issued at a <sup>*</sup>discount, or the increase in market value happens, is called the _increase time_ for that interest. </dd> </dl></dl>

725-160  What is the nature of a direct value shift?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>direct value shift has 2 aspects.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Overall, it consists of: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the decreases in market value of the down interests; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the issue at a <sup>*</sup>discount of the up interests covered by

subsection 725-145(2); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the increases in market value of the up interests covered by subsection

725-145(3).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>This Division also proceeds on the basis that the <sup>*</sup>direct value

shift is from _each_ of the <sup>*</sup>down interests to _each_ of

the <sup>*</sup>up interests.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

725-165  If market value decrease or increase is only partly attributable to the scheme

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If it is reasonable to conclude that an increase or decrease in market value,

or the issuing of an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest at a

<sup>*</sup>discount, is only partly caused by the doing of the one or more

things under the <sup>*</sup>scheme, this Division applies to the increase,

decrease, or issue at a discount, to that extent only.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;725-C&#151;Consequences of a direct value shift 

Table of sections

General

725-205	Consequences depend on character of down interests and up interests
 725-210	Consequences for down interests depend on pre-shift gains and losses

Special cases

725-220	Neutral direct value shifts
 725-225	Issue of bonus shares or units
 725-230	Off-market buy-backs

General
 725-205  Consequences depend on character of down interests and up interests

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The consequences for you of the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift depend on

the character of the <sup>*</sup>down interests and <sup>*</sup>up interests of

which you are an <sup>*</sup>affected owner.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>There are consequences for all your <sup>*</sup>down interests and <sup>*</sup>up interests in their character as <sup>*</sup>CGT assets. However, some of them may also be <sup>*</sup>trading stock or <sup>*</sup>revenue assets. There are additional consequences for those interests in their character as trading stock or revenue assets. </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, you may own a down interest that is a CGT

asset and a revenue asset. 	Sections&#160;725-240 to 725-255 set out the consequences for you of a shift in value from that interest in its character as a CGT asset. The cost base of the asset will be decreased, which will affect the calculation of a capital gain when a CGT event happens to the interest. 	Section&#160;725-320 sets out the consequences for you of a shift in value from that interest in its character as a revenue asset. The adjustment made under that section will affect the calculation of any profit on the sale of the interest. 	Any overlap between the capital gain and the profit realised on the sale of the interest is then dealt with under section&#160;118-20\. 	In some instances, the direct value shift may result in a taxing event generating a gain for you in the income year in which the shift happens. That gain will be both a capital gain (because the down interest can be characterised as a CGT asset) and an increase in your assessable income (because the down interest can be characterised as a revenue asset). Again, any overlap is dealt with under section&#160;118-20\.  </dl></dl>

725-210  Consequences for down interests depend on pre-shift gains and losses

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The consequences for a <sup>*</sup>down interest also depend on whether it

has a <sup>*</sup>pre-shift gain or a <sup>*</sup>pre-shift loss.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>It has a _pre-shift_ _gain_ if, immediately before the <sup>*</sup>decrease time, its market value was _greater than_ its <sup>*</sup>adjustable value.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>It has a _pre-shift_ _loss_ if, immediately before the <sup>*</sup>decrease time, its market value was _equal to or less than_ its <sup>*</sup>adjustable value. </dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 725-220.]_

Special cases
 725-220  Neutral direct value shifts

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The consequences are different if the total decrease in market value of

your <sup>*</sup>down interests is equal to the sum of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the total increase in market value of your <sup>*</sup>up interests; and</dd>

(b)	the total <sup>*</sup>discounts given to you on the issue of your

up interests.

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In that case, this Subdivision and Subdivisions&#160;725-D to 725-F apply

to you as if the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>consisted only of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the decreases in market value of your <sup>*</sup>down interests; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the issue at a <sup>*</sup>discount of your <sup>*</sup>up interests

covered by subsection 725-145(2); and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the increases in market value of your up interests covered by subsection

725-145(3); and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>were from each of your down interests to each of your up interests.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>This section has effect despite section&#160;725-160.

</dd> </dl></dl>

725-225  Issue of bonus shares or units

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The consequences are different if you are an <sup>*</sup>affected owner of

<sup>*</sup>up interests (the _bonus interests_) that the target

entity issues to you, at a <sup>*</sup>discount, under the <sup>*</sup>scheme,

in relation to <sup>*</sup>down interests (the _original interests_) of which you are an affected owner.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Effect of treatment under subsection 130-20(3)_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>To the extent that the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift is _to_ the

bonus interests _from_ original interests in relation to which the target

entity issued bonus interests to which:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>subsection 130-20(3) applies (because none of them is a dividend or

otherwise assessable income); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>item&#160;1 of the table in that subsection applies (because the original

interests are post-CGT assets);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

these paragraphs apply:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the respective <sup>*</sup>cost bases and <sup>*</sup>reduced cost bases

of those original interests are not reduced;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the bonus interests referred to in subsection&#160;(1) do not give rise to

a <sup>*</sup>taxing event generating a gain for you under the table in

section&#160;725-245 on any of those original interests.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>To the extent that the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift is _from_ the

original interests _to_ bonus interests to which subsection 130-20(3)

applies (because none of them is a dividend or otherwise assessable income) and:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>item&#160;1 of the table in that subsection applies (because the original

interests are post-CGT assets); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>item&#160;2 of that table applies (because the original interests are

pre-CGT assets and an amount has been paid for the bonus interests that you

were required to pay); 

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the respective <sup>*</sup>cost bases and <sup>*</sup>reduced cost bases of those bonus interests are not uplifted.

_Effect of treatment under subsection 6BA(3) of the Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>To the extent that the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift is _to_ the

bonus interests _from_ original interests in relation to which the target

entity issued bonus interests to which subsection 6BA(3) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies (either because they are shares issued for no

consideration and none of them is a dividend or because they qualify for the

intercorporate dividend rebate):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the respective <sup>*</sup>adjustable values of those original interests,

in their character as <sup>*</sup>trading stock or <sup>*</sup>revenue assets,

are not reduced; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bonus interests referred to in subsection&#160;(1) do not give rise to

a <sup>*</sup>taxing event generating a gain for you under the table in

section&#160;725-335 on any of those original interests.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>To the extent that the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift is _from_ the

original interests to bonus interests to which subsection 6BA(3) of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies, the respective

<sup>*</sup>adjustable values of those bonus interests of which you are an

affected owner, in their character as trading stock or revenue assets, are not

uplifted.

</dd> </dl></dl>

725-230  Off-market buy-backs

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The consequences are different if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a decrease in the market value of a <sup>*</sup>down interest of which you

are an <sup>*</sup>affected owner is reasonably attributable to the target

entity proposing to buy back that interest for less than its market value;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the target entity does buy back that down interest; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>subsection 159GZZZQ(2) of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ treats

you as having received the down interest's market value worked out as if the

buy-back had not occurred and was never proposed to occur.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the <sup>*</sup>down interest is not

reduced, and there is no <sup>*</sup>taxing event generating a gain.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The down interest is not dealt with here because it is

already dealt with in Division&#160;16K of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Also, to the extent that the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift is from the

<sup>*</sup>down interest to <sup>*</sup>up interests of which you are an

<sup>*</sup>affected owner, uplifts in the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the

up interests are worked out under either or both of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>item&#160;8 of the table in subsection 725-250(2); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>item&#160;9 of the table in subsection 725-335(3);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as if the down interest were one owned by another affected owner.

Subdivision&#160;725-D&#151;Consequences for down interest or up interest as CGT asset 

Table of sections

725-240	CGT consequences; meaning of _adjustable value_
 725-245	Table of _taxing events generating a gain_ for interests as CGT assets
 725-250	Table of consequences for adjustable values of interests as CGT assets
 725-255	Multiple CGT consequences for the same down interest or up interest

725-240  CGT consequences; meaning of adjustable value

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The CGT consequences for you of a <sup>*</sup>direct value shift are of

one or more of these 3 kinds:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>there are one or more <sup>*</sup>taxing events generating a gain for

<sup>*</sup>down interests of which you are an affected owner (see

subsection&#160;(2));</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>cost base and <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of down

interests of which you are an <sup>*</sup>affected owner are reduced (see

subsection&#160;(3));</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the cost base and reduced cost base of <sup>*</sup>up interests of which

you are an affected owner are uplifted (see subsection&#160;(4)).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If there is a taxing event generating a gain, CGT event K8

happens. See section&#160;104-240.

 </dl></dl>

_Taxing event generating a gain_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>To work out:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>whether under the table in section&#160;725-245 there is a

<sup>*</sup>taxing event generating a gain for you on a <sup>*</sup>down

interest; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if so, the amount of the gain;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

assume that the _adjustable value_ from time to time of that or any other <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in the <sup>*</sup>target entity is its <sup>*</sup>cost base.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, for that purpose the question whether the

interest has a pre-shift gain or a pre-shift loss is determined on the basis

that the interest's adjustable value is its cost base.

 </dl></dl>

_Reduction or uplift of cost base and reduced cost base_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>cost base and the <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of a

<sup>*</sup>down interest are reduced at the <sup>*</sup>decrease time to the

extent that section&#160;725-250 provides for the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value

of the interest to be reduced.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>cost base and the <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of an <sup>*</sup>up interest are uplifted at the <sup>*</sup>increase time to the extent that section&#160;725-250 provides for the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the interest to be uplifted.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>However, the <sup>*</sup>cost base or <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base is _uplifted_ only to the extent that the amount of the uplift is still reflected in the market value of the interest when a later <sup>*</sup>CGT event happens to the interest.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>To work out: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>whether the <sup>*</sup>cost base or <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of the

interest is reduced or uplifted; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if so, by how much;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

assume that:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the _adjustable value_ from time to time of that or any other

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in the <sup>*</sup>target entity is its

cost base or reduced cost base, as appropriate; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the interest is an <sup>*</sup>up interest because it was issued at a

<sup>*</sup>discount&#151;the _adjustable value_ of the interest

immediately before it was issued was its cost base or reduced cost base, as

appropriate, when it was issued.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For example, for that purpose the question whether the

interest has a pre-shift gain or a pre-shift loss is determined on the basis

that the interest's adjustable value is its cost base or reduced cost base, as

appropriate.

 </dl></dl>

_Reductions and uplifts also apply to pre-CGT assets_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>A reduction or uplift occurs regardless of whether the entity that owns

the interest <sup>*</sup>acquired it before, on or after 20&#160;September 1985.

</dd> </dl></dl>

725-245  Table of taxing events generating a gain for interests as CGT assets

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		To the extent that the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift is from

<sup>*</sup>down interests of which you are an <sup>*</sup>affected owner, and

that are specified in an item in the table, to <sup>*</sup>up interests

specified in that item, those up interests give rise to a _taxing event generating a gain_ for you on each of those down interests. The gain is

worked out under section&#160;725-365.

 </dl></dl>

725-250  Table of consequences for adjustable values of interests as CGT assets

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The table in subsection&#160;(2) sets out consequences of the

<sup>*</sup>direct value shift for the <sup>*</sup>adjustable values of

<sup>*</sup>down interests and <sup>*</sup>up interests of which you are an

<sup>*</sup>affected owner, in their character as <sup>*</sup>CGT assets.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>To the extent that the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift is from <sup>*</sup>down interests specified in an item in the table to <sup>*</sup>up interests specified in that item: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of each of those down interests is

decreased by the amount worked out under the section (if any) specified for the

down interests in the last column of that item; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the adjustable value of each of those <sup>*</sup>up interests is uplifted

by the amount worked out under the section (if any) specified for the up

interests in that column.

</dd>
