    <div>There must be 2 or more <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners who:</div>
    <div>(a) at some time during that period, because of the same test in section&#160;727-410, have <sup>*</sup>ultimate stakes, of percentages totalling at least 80%, in one of the trusts; and 
(b) at that or a different time during that period, because of that same test, have <sup>*</sup>ultimate stakes, of percentages totalling at least 80%, in the other trust</div>
    <div>Also, subsection&#160;(2) of this section must be satisfied</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a company and a <sup>*</sup>fixed trust</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>There must be 2 or more <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners who:</div>
    <div>(a) at some time during that period, because of the same test in section&#160;727-405, have <sup>*</sup>ultimate stakes, of percentages totalling at least 80%, in the company; and 
(b) at that or a different time during that period, because of the same test in section&#160;727-410, have <sup>*</sup>ultimate stakes, of percentages totalling at least 80%, in the trust</div>
    <div>Also, subsection&#160;(2) of this section must be satisfied</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>4</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a company and a <sup>*</sup>non-fixed trust</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>There must be 2 or more <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners:</div>
    <div>(a) each of whom <sup>*</sup>controls (for value shifting purposes) the non-fixed trust because of section&#160;727-365 at the same time during that period; and 
(b) who, at that or a different time during that period, have <sup>*</sup>ultimate stakes, of percentages totalling at least 80%, in the company because of the same test in section&#160;727-405</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>5</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a <sup>*</sup>fixed trust and a <sup>*</sup>non-fixed trust</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>There must be 2 or more <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners:</div>
    <div>(a) each of whom <sup>*</sup>controls (for value shifting purposes) the non-fixed trust because of section&#160;727-365 at the same time during that period; and 
(b) who, at that or a different time during that period, have <sup>*</sup>ultimate stakes, of percentages totalling at least 80%, in the fixed trust because of the same test in section&#160;727-410</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>_Additional Back to Top condition about profile of percentage ultimate stakes held by 2 or more ultimate owners_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In order to satisfy the test in item&#160;1, 2 or 3 in the table in

subsection&#160;(1), at least one of subsections&#160;(3), (4) and (5) must be

satisfied.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>For at least one of the <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners referred to in that item, the percentage of the <sup>*</sup>ultimate stake that owner has as mentioned in paragraph&#160;(a) in the last column of that item must be at least 40%, and so must the percentage of the ultimate stake that owner has as mentioned in paragraph&#160;(b) in the last column of that item.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Alternatively, for _each_ of those <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners, the percentage of the <sup>*</sup>ultimate stake that owner has as mentioned in that paragraph&#160;(a) must be the same as the percentage of the ultimate stake that owner has as mentioned in that paragraph&#160;(b).</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>Alternatively, the number of those <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners must not exceed 16\. </dd> </dl></dl>

727-405  Ultimate stake of a particular percentage in a company

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section sets out 3 tests of whether an entity has an _ultimate stake_ of a particular percentage (the _test percentage_) in

a company.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	In applying the tests, follow the rules in

section&#160;727-415.

 </dl></dl>

_Voting power_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The first test is that, after tracing, to the <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners

who ultimately hold it, the direct and indirect ownership of all

<sup>*</sup>shares in the company that carry the right to exercise voting power

in the company, that ownership is held by the entity to the extent of the test

percentage of that voting power.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Dividends_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The second test is that, after tracing, to the <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners

who ultimately hold it, the direct and indirect ownership of all

<sup>*</sup>shares in the company that carry the right to receive any dividends

that the company may pay, that ownership is held by the entity to the extent of

the test percentage of those dividends.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Capital distributions_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The third test is that, after tracing, to the <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners

who ultimately hold it, the direct and indirect ownership of all

<sup>*</sup>shares in the company that carry the right to receive any

distribution of capital of the company, that ownership is held by the entity to

the extent of the test percentage of the distribution.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Certain shares ignored_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>In tracing the ownership of <sup>*</sup>shares in a company, ignore

<sup>*</sup>shares whose <sup>*</sup>dividends can reasonably be regarded as

being equivalent to the payment of interest on a loan having regard to:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>how the dividends are calculated; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the conditions applying to the payment of the dividends; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any other relevant matters.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-410  Ultimate stake of a particular percentage in a fixed trust

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section sets out 2 tests of whether an entity has an _ultimate stake_ of a particular percentage (the _test percentage_) in

a <sup>*</sup>fixed trust.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	In applying the tests, follow the rules in

section&#160;727-415.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Income distributions_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The first test is that, after tracing, to the <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners

who ultimately hold them, the direct and indirect rights to receive

distributions of trust income, those rights are held by the entity to the

extent of the test percentage of each such distribution.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Capital distributions_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The second test is that, after tracing, to the <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners

who ultimately hold them, the direct and indirect rights to receive

distributions of trust capital, those rights are held by the entity to the

extent of the test percentage of each such distribution.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-415  Rules for tracing

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>In applying sections&#160;727-400, 727-405 and 727-410, follow the rules

in this section.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Interposed entities_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Tracing is to be done through any interposed entities.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Ownership or rights held jointly_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If some of the ownership or rights of a particular kind in relation to a

company or trust are held by 2 or more entities jointly or in common, each of

the entities is treated as holding a proportion of the ownership or rights so

held. The proportion is to be worked out on a reasonable basis, so that the

total of the proportions equals the total of the ownership or rights so held.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Ownership or rights held by associate_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If, at a particular time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>ultimate owner is an <sup>*</sup>associate of another

ultimate owner; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the associate ultimately holds some of the ownership or rights of a

particular kind in relation to a company or trust;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then, in determining whether the other ultimate owner is one of 2 or more ultimate owners because of whom the conditions in an item in the table in section&#160;727-400 are satisfied, the ownership or rights of that kind in relation to the company or trust held by the associate at that time:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>to the extent of a particular percentage, may be treated as being instead

held by the other ultimate owner; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>to the extent so treated, cannot be treated as being instead held by any

other ultimate owner of whom the first ultimate owner is an associate.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If one or more applications of subsection&#160;(4) are necessary to

establish that an <sup>*</sup>ultimate owner is one of 2 or more ultimate

owners because of whom the conditions in an item in the table in

section&#160;727-400 are satisfied, that subsection must be applied accordingly.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;727-F&#151;Consequences of an indirect value shift
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;727-F
 727-450  What this Subdivision is about

This Subdivision tells you:

*	which method to use to work out the consequences of an indirect value shift for equity or loan interests, and indirect equity or loan interests, in the losing entity and in the gaining entity; and

*	which interests, and which owners, are affected. 

Table of sections

Operative provisions

727-455	Consequences of the indirect value shift

Affected interests

727-460	_Affected interests_ in the losing entity

<center>Back to Top</center>
 727-465	_Affected interests_ in the gaining entity
 727-470	Exceptions
 727-520	_Equity or loan interest_ and related terms
 727-525	_Indirect equity or loan interest_

Affected owners

727-530	Who are the _affected owners_

Choices about method to be used

727-550	Choosing the adjustable value method
 727-555	Giving other affected owners information about the choice

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 727-455  Consequences of the indirect value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The consequences (if any) of an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift must be

worked out using the <sup>*</sup>realisation time method unless the

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value method is chosen in accordance with

section&#160;727-550.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Later provisions of this Subdivision set out the interests

to which those consequences apply (see sections&#160;727-460 to 727-525), which

are in turn determined by who are the affected owners (see

section&#160;727-530).

 </dl></dl>

Affected interests
 727-460  Affected interests in the losing entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		These are the _affected interests_ in the <sup>*</sup>losing

entity:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest that an <sup>*</sup>affected

owner owns in the losing entity immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each equity or loan interest that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an affected owner owns in another affected owner immediately before the

IVS time; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is an <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest in the losing entity;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

(except one covered by an exception in section&#160;727-470).

727-465  Affected interests in the gaining entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity

is a company or trust (except one listed in section&#160;727-125 (about

superannuation entities)), these are the _affected interests_ in

the gaining entity:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest that an <sup>*</sup>affected

owner owns in the gaining entity immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each equity or loan interest that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an affected owner owns in another affected owner immediately before the

IVS time; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is an <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest in the gaining entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

(except one covered by an exception in section&#160;727-470).

727-470  Exceptions

_Mere active participants_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest that an <sup>*</sup>active

participant in the <sup>*</sup>scheme owns in another active participant

immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time is not an <sup>*</sup>affected

interest in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or in the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity

unless one of the active participants is also covered by 1, 2, 3 or 4 in the

table in subsection 727-530(1) (about who is an affected owner).

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Entity that is eligible to be an STS taxpayer, or satisfies the maximum net asset value test for small business relief_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest that an entity (the

_owner_) owns immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time is not an

<sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or in the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity if the owner:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is eligible to be an <sup>*</sup>STS taxpayer for each income year that

includes any of the <sup>*</sup>IVS period; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>would satisfy the maximum net asset value test in section&#160;152-15

throughout the <sup>*</sup>IVS period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the owner is not in existence for part of the <sup>*</sup>IVS period,

disregard that part in applying subsection&#160;(2).

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Interests in superannuation entities not covered_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in an <sup>*</sup>affected owner is

not an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or in the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity if the affected owner is an entity listed in

section&#160;727-125 (about superannuation entities) in relation to the income

year in which the <sup>*</sup>IVS time happens.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 727-520.]_

727-520  Equity or loan interest and related terms

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An _equity or loan interest_ in an entity is a

<sup>*</sup>primary interest, or a <sup>*</sup>secondary interest, in the

entity.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A _primary interest_ in an entity is a <sup>*</sup>primary equity interest, or a <sup>*</sup>primary loan interest, in the entity.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The meaning of _primary equity interest_ in an entity is set out in the table. </dd> </dl></dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Primary equity interests</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Item</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>In the case of this kind of entity:</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Primary equity interest means:</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a company</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a <sup>*</sup>share in the company; or 
an interest as joint owner (including as tenant in common) of a <sup>*</sup>share in the company</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a trust</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>any of these:</div>
    <div>(a) an interest in the trust income or trust capital; or 
(b) any other interest in the trust; or 
(c) an interest as joint owner (including as tenant in common) of an interest covered by paragraph&#160;(a) or (b)</div>

  </td>
</tr></table><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A _primary loan interest_ in an entity is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>loan to the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an interest as joint owner (including as tenant in common) of a loan to

the entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A _secondary interest_ in an entity is a <sup>*</sup>secondary

equity interest, or a <sup>*</sup>secondary loan interest, in the entity.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>A _secondary equity interest_ in an entity is a right or option: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to<sup> *</sup>acquire an existing <sup>*</sup>primary equity interest in

the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to have the entity issue a new primary equity interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>A _secondary loan interest_ in an entity is a right or option:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to <sup>*</sup>acquire an existing <sup>*</sup>primary loan interest in

the entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to have the entity issue a new primary loan interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-525  Indirect equity or loan interest

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in an entity is an _indirect equity or loan interest_ in another entity if, and only if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first entity owns an equity or loan interest in the other entity; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first entity owns an equity or loan interest that is an indirect

equity or loan interest in the other entity because of one or more other

applications of this section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 727-530.]_

Affected owners
 727-530  Who are the affected owners

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The table sets out the _affected owners_ for the

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Affected owners</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Item</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>In this case:</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The affected owners include:</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>At least one condition in section&#160;727-105 (ultimate controller test) is satisfied</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>each <sup>*</sup>ultimate controller because of which a condition in that section is satisfied; and 
each entity that, at a time during the <sup>*</sup>IVS period when such an ultimate controller <sup>*</sup>controlled (for value shifting purposes) the <i>losing</i>entity, was an <sup>*</sup>intermediate controller of the <i>losing</i>entity; and 
each entity that, at a time during the IVS period when such an ultimate controller controlled (for value shifting purposes) the <i>gaining</i>entity, was an intermediate controller of the <i>gaining</i>entity</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The conditions in section&#160;727-110 (common-ownership nexus test) are satisfied in respect of:</div>
    <div>(a) one or more times; or 
(b) one or more sets of 2 times</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>each <sup>*</sup>ultimate owner who is one of 2 or more ultimate owners because of whom the condition in the applicable item of that table is satisfied in respect of any of those times; and 
each entity through which ownership or rights are traced to such an ultimate owner in applying the applicable item of that table in respect of any of those times</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Any case</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the <sup>*</sup>losing entity and the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>4</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Any case</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>each entity that, at any time after the <sup>*</sup>scheme was entered into, is an <sup>*</sup>associate of an entity that is an affected owner because of item&#160;1, 2 or 3 of this table</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>5</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Any case</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>each <sup>*</sup>active participant in the <sup>*</sup>scheme</div>

  </td>
</tr></table><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An entity is an _intermediate controller_ of another entity

if, and only if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first entity <sup>*</sup>controls (for value shifting purposes) the

other entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first entity is <sup>*</sup>controlled (for value shifting purposes)

by an <sup>*</sup>ultimate controller of the other entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Active participants (if both losing and gaining entities are closely held)_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An entity (the _first entity_) is an _active participant_ in the <sup>*</sup>scheme if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at some time during the <sup>*</sup>IVS period, neither the losing entity

nor the gaining entity has 300 or more members (in the case of a company) or

300 or more beneficiaries (in the case of a trust); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the first entity:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>actively participated in, or directly facilitated, the entering into of

the <sup>*</sup>scheme; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>at some time during the <sup>*</sup>IVS period actively participated in,

or directly facilitated, the carrying out of the scheme;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		(whether or not it did so at the direction of some other entity); and

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>at some time during the <sup>*</sup>IVS period, the first entity owned:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in the losing entity or in the

gaining entity; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest in the losing entity or

in the gaining entity; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the first entity is neither the losing entity nor the gaining entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsections 727-110(2) and (3) contain rules about when an

entity is treated as having or not having 300 or more members or beneficiaries.

 </dl></dl>

Choices about method to be used
 727-550  Choosing the adjustable value method

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section sets out rules for:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>choosing to use the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value method to work out the

consequences of an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>choosing (when using the adjustable value method) _not_ to work out

on a <sup>*</sup>loss-focussed basis the reductions in the

<sup>*</sup>adjustable values of <sup>*</sup>affected interests.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Who makes the choice_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The choice must be made in accordance with the table.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Who makes the choice</div>

  </th>
</tr>

  </td>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>jointly by the <sup>*</sup>ultimate owners because of whom the condition in the applicable item of the table in section&#160;727-400 is satisfied</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Item&#160;1 does not apply, and there is an entity:</div>
    <div>(a) who is the sole <sup>*</sup>ultimate controller because of whom the conditions in section&#160;727-105 (ultimate controller test) are satisfied; or 
(b) who would be that sole ultimate controller if sections&#160;727-355 to 727-375 were applied ignoring that entity's <sup>*</sup>associates</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>that entity</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Neither of items&#160;1 and 2 applies</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>jointly by the 2 or more <sup>*</sup>ultimate controllers because of whom the conditions in section&#160;727-105 (ultimate controller test) are satisfied</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>_When Back to Top choice must be made_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The choice must be made within 2 years after the _first_

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to an <sup>*</sup>affected interest

at or after the IVS time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Choice binds all affected owners_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The choice binds all <sup>*</sup>affected owners for the

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-555  Giving other affected owners information about the choice

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An entity that makes a choice under section&#160;727-550 (including a

choice made jointly with one or more other entities) must inform all entities

that it knows to be <sup>*</sup>affected owners for the <sup>*</sup>indirect

value shift about the content of the choice. The entity must do so in writing

within one month after making the choice.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Penalty:	30 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a choice under section&#160;727-550 is made jointly by 2 or more entities;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>one of the entities complies with subsection&#160;(1);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

no other entity need comply with that subsection in relation to that choice.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If an <sup>*</sup>affected owner for an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift

has reason to believe that an entity may have made a choice under

section&#160;727-550 (including a choice made jointly with one or more other

entities), the affected owner may give the entity a written notice asking

whether the entity has made such a choice.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Within one month after receiving a notice under subsection&#160;(3), an entity must inform the <sup>*</sup>affected owner in writing whether the entity has made a choice under section&#160;727-550 and, if so, about the content of the choice. </dd> </dl></dl>

Penalty:	30 penalty units.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may extend the period for complying with a provision of

this section.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;727-G&#151;The realisation time method
 727-600  What this Subdivision is about

Under the realisation time method:

*	losses on realisation of affected interests in the losing entity are reduced; and

*	gains on realisation of affected interests in the gaining entity are reduced, within limits worked out by reference to the reductions in losses on affected interests in the losing entity; and

*	certain 95% services indirect value shifts are disregarded. 

This Subdivision also explains how its reduction of a loss or gain affects CGT assets, trading stock and revenue assets.

Operative provisions
 727-610  Consequences of indirect value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Subdivision sets out the _realisation time method_ of

working out the consequences (if any) of an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If those consequences are to be worked out using that method, this Subdivision applies to each <sup>*</sup>realisation event: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>by which a loss would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised

for income tax purposes; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that happens to an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>losing

entity; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that is the first realisation event that happens to that interest at or

after the <sup>*</sup>IVS time; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>that happens:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the amount of the indirect value shift is $500,000 or more&#151;at any time

after the IVS time; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;within 4 years after the IVS time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>those consequences are to be worked out using that method; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity is a company or trust (except one listed in

section&#160;727-125 (about superannuation entities)) immediately before the

<sup>*</sup>IVS time;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

this Subdivision applies to each <sup>*</sup>realisation event:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>by which a gain would, apart from this Division, be<sup> *</sup>realised

for income tax purposes; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>that happens to an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>that is the first realisation event that happens to that interest at or

after the IVS time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The consequences for the <sup>*</sup>affected interest depend on its

character. There are consequences for the interest in its character as a

<sup>*</sup>CGT asset. However, if the interest is also <sup>*</sup>trading

stock or a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset, there are additional consequences for it

in that character.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>In working out the consequences for an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or <sup>*</sup>gaining entity, in the interest's character as <sup>*</sup>trading stock, a <sup>*</sup>realisation event is disregarded for the purposes of identifying under paragraph&#160;(2)(c) or (3)(e) the first realisation event that happens to that interest at or after the <sup>*</sup>IVS time, if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the realisation event consists of the ending of an income year; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>value of the interest as trading stock on hand of an

entity at the end of the income year is the interest's <sup>*</sup>cost; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the interest became part of the entity's trading stock on hand during that

income year, or the value of the interest as trading stock of the entity on

hand at the start of the income year was also the interest's cost.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

727-615  Reduction of loss on realisation event for affected interest in losing entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If this Subdivision applies to a <sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens

to an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity, a loss

that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax

purposes by the event is reduced by an amount that is reasonable having regard

to:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a reasonable estimate of the amount (if any) by which the

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift has reduced the interest's market value; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the interest is also an affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>gaining

entity&#151;a reasonable estimate of the extent (if any) to which the interest's

market value at the time of the realisation event still reflects the effect of

the indirect value shift on the market value of <sup>*</sup>equity or loan

interests in the gaining entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-620  Reduction of gain on realisation event for affected interest in gaining entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If this Subdivision applies to a <sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens

to an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity, a gain

that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax

purposes by the event is reduced by an amount that is reasonable having regard

to:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a reasonable estimate of the amount (if any) by which the

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift has increased the interest's market value;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a reasonable estimate of the extent (if any) to which the interest's

market value at the time of the realisation event still reflects the effect of

the indirect value shift on the market value of <sup>*</sup>equity or loan

interests in the gaining entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-625  Total gain reductions not to exceed total loss reductions

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section ensures that the total (_total gain reductions_)

of the amounts by which section&#160;727-620 reduces gains <sup>*</sup>realised

for income tax purposes by <sup>*</sup>realisation events happening at the same

time does not exceed the total (_total loss reductions_) of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amounts by which section&#160;727-615 reduces losses that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax

purposes by <sup>*</sup>realisation events happening before or at that time;

and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>have not already been taken into account in a previous application of

this section; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amounts by which section&#160;727-850 (as applying to the

<sup>*</sup>scheme from which the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift results)

reduces losses that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>would, apart from this Division, be realised for income tax purposes by

realisation events happening before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time to

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests, or <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan

interests, in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>have not already been taken into account in a previous application of

this section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If, apart from this section, the total gain reductions would exceed the

total loss reductions, the amount by which section&#160;727-620 reduces each of

the gains is itself reduced by the amount worked out using this formula:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1224.gif)</sub>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of the formula:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_number of interests_ means the number of <sup>*</sup>affected

interests in the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity to which <sup>*</sup>realisation

events happened at that time.

 </dl></dl>

727-630  How cap in section&#160;727-625 applies if affected interest is also trading stock or a revenue asset

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section affects how to work out the total gain reductions and the

total loss reductions for the purposes of section&#160;727-625 if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>realisation event covered by that section happens to an

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest, or to an <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or

loan interest, in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or in the <sup>*</sup>gaining

entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the interest is also <sup>*</sup>trading stock or a <sup>*</sup>revenue

asset at the time of the event.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Trading stock_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In the case of an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest, or an

<sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest, in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity

that is <sup>*</sup>trading stock at that time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) by which section&#160;727-615 or 727-850 reduces a

loss worked out under section&#160;977-25 or 977-30 (about realisation events

for trading stock) that would, apart from this Division, be

<sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the event is taken into

account; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) by which section&#160;727-615 or 727-850 reduces a

loss worked out under section&#160;977-10 (about realisation events for CGT

assets) that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for

income tax purposes by the event is _not_ taken into account;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

in working out the total loss reductions.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In the case of an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>gaining

entity that is <sup>*</sup>trading stock at that time:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) by which section&#160;727-620 reduces a gain worked

out under section&#160;977-35 or 977-40 (about realisation events for trading

stock) that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income

tax purposes by the event is taken into account; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) by which section&#160;727-620 reduces a gain worked

out under section&#160;977-15 (about realisation events for CGT assets) that

would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax

purposes by the event is _not_ taken into account;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

in working out the total gain reductions.

_Revenue asset_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>In the case of an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest, or an

<sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest, in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity

that is a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset at that time, the greater of the following

is taken into account in working out the total loss reductions:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) by which section&#160;727-615 or 727-850 reduces a

loss worked out under section&#160;977-55 (about realisation events for revenue

assets) that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for

income tax purposes by the event;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) by which section&#160;727-615 or 727-850 reduces a

loss worked out under section&#160;977-10 (about realisation events for CGT

assets) that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for

income tax purposes by the event.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>In the case of an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>gaining

entity that is a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset at that time, the greater of the

following amounts is taken into account in working out the total gain

reductions:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) by which section&#160;727-620 reduces a gain worked

out under section&#160;977-55 (about realisation events for revenue assets)

that would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax

purposes by the event;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) by which section&#160;727-620 reduces a gain worked

out under section&#160;977-15 (about realisation events for CGT assets) that

would, apart from this Division, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax

purposes by the event.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-635  Splitting an equity or loan interest

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or

in the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity is split into 2 or more equity or loan

interests at or after the <sup>*</sup>IVS time:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each of the 2 or more interests inherits whatever characteristics would

have been relevant to applying this Subdivision to the first interest if the

split had not happened; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>those characteristics include characteristics the first interest has

inherited because of any other application or applications of this section or

section&#160;727-640; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if a characteristic of the first interest involves an amount or quantity,

the amount or quantity for that characteristic as inherited by each of the 2 or

more interests is a reasonable proportion of the amount or quantity for that

characteristic of the first interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-640  Merging equity or loan interests

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If 2 or more <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests (the _original interests_) in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or in the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity are merged into 1 or more <sup>*</sup>equity or loan

interests (the _new interests_) at or after the <sup>*</sup>IVS

time:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each of the new interests inherits whatever characteristics would have

been relevant to applying this Subdivision to the original interests if the

merging had not happened; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>those characteristics include characteristics inherited by any of the

original interests because of any other application or applications of this

section or section&#160;727-635; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if a characteristic of any of the original interests involves an amount or

quantity, the amount or quantity for that characteristic as inherited by any of

the new interests is a reasonable proportion of the amount or quantity for that

characteristic of the original interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-645  Effect of CGT roll-over

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>this Subdivision applies to a <sup>*</sup>realisation event that is a

<sup>*</sup>CGT event that happens to an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the

<sup>*</sup>losing entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-615 reduces a loss that would, apart from this Division,

be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the CGT event; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>there is a roll-over for the CGT event;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the interest's <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base at the time of the CGT event is taken to have been reduced by the amount by which section&#160;727-615 reduces that loss, but is so taken only for the purposes of working out:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the interest's reduced cost base, from time to time after the roll-over,

for the entity that <sup>*</sup>acquired the interest because of the CGT event;

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>in the case of a <sup>*</sup>replacement-asset roll-over&#151;the reduced cost

base of the replacement CGT asset, from time to time after the roll-over, for

the entity that <sup>*</sup>disposed of the interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Because of the roll-over, the loss reduction under

section&#160;727-615 will have no tax effect. This subsection ensures that the

loss reduction is passed on, through the reduction in reduced cost base, to

prevent or reduce a loss arising on a later CGT event.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>this Subdivision applies to a <sup>*</sup>realisation event that is a

<sup>*</sup>CGT event that happens to an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-620 reduces a gain that would, apart from this Division,

be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the CGT event; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>there is a roll-over for the CGT event;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the interest's <sup>*</sup>cost base at the time of the CGT event is taken to have been uplifted by the amount by which section&#160;727-620 reduces that gain, but is so taken only for the purposes of working out:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the interest's cost base, from time to time after the roll-over, for the

entity that <sup>*</sup>acquired the interest because of the CGT event; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>in the case of a <sup>*</sup>replacement-asset roll-over&#151;the cost base of

the replacement CGT asset, from time to time after the roll-over, for the

entity that <sup>*</sup>disposed of the interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Because of the roll-over, the gain reduction under

section&#160;727-620 will have no tax effect. This subsection ensures that the

gain reduction is passed on, through the uplift in cost base, to prevent or

reduce a gain arising on a later CGT event.

 </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 727-700.]_

Further exclusion for certain 95% services indirect value shifts if realisation time method must be used
 727-700  When 95% services indirect value shift is excluded

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift is a <sup>*</sup>95% services

indirect value shift, this Subdivision does not apply to a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>happens to an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>losing

entity that is owned by an entity (the _owner_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is covered by subsection 727-610(2);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

unless:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the conditions in section&#160;727-705 are met for the indirect value

shift; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the conditions in section&#160;727-710, 727-715 or 727-720 are met for the

indirect value shift and for that realisation event.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift is a _95% services indirect value shift_ if, and only if, to the extent of at least 95% of their total

market value, the <sup>*</sup>greater benefits consist entirely of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a right to have services that are covered by section&#160;727-240 provided

directly by the <sup>*</sup>losing entity to the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>services that are covered by section&#160;727-240 and have been, are

being, or are to be, so provided;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

or both.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>This section does not limit any other exclusion in this Subdivision or in

Subdivision&#160;727-C.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

95% services indirect value shifts that are not excluded
 727-705  Another provision of the income tax law affects amount related to services by at least $100,000

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The conditions in this section are met if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>losing entity or the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity lodges an

<sup>*</sup>income tax return for an income year during some or all of which

the owner owned the interest; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a provision of this Act:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>reduces or excludes an amount that is included in the return; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>increases an amount that is so included; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>includes an amount not included in the return;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		for the purposes of working out the taxable income, a <sup>*</sup>tax loss,

or a <sup>*</sup>net capital loss, of that entity for that income year; and

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the amount is related to the right mentioned in paragraph 727-700(2)(a),

or to some or all of the services mentioned in paragraph 727-700(2)(a) or (b),

from the point of view of the losing entity providing the services or of the

gaining entity receiving them; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the amount is so reduced or increased&#151;the reduction or increase is at

least $100,000; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>if the amount is so excluded or included&#151;the amount is at least $100,000;

and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>at some time after the return is lodged, the entity that lodged it is

aware, or ought reasonably to be aware, of the reduction, exclusion, increase

or inclusion.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Example:	If the Commissioner has notified an entity affected by a

determination under Part&#160;IVA of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_,

the entity ought reasonably to be aware of the effect of the determination.

 </dl></dl>

727-710  Ongoing or recent service arrangement reduces value of losing entity by at least $100,000

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Either or both of these must be true:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>when the <sup>*</sup>realisation event mentioned in subsection 727-700(1)

happens, some or all of the services mentioned in paragraph 727-700(2)(a) or

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>have not yet been provided; or</dd></dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>some or all of those services have been provided in the income year (of

the <sup>*</sup>losing entity) in which the realisation event happens, or in

the previous income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>It must be reasonable to conclude that the total (the _total market value_) of the market values, immediately before the

<sup>*</sup>realisation event, of <sup>*</sup>primary interests in the

<sup>*</sup>losing entity then owned by <sup>*</sup>affected owners is less

than it would have been if none of the following had happened:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>95% services indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>all other <sup>*</sup>predominantly-services indirect value shifts that

satisfy subsection&#160;(1) (or that would satisfy it if they were

<sup>*</sup>95% services indirect value shifts).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>It must also be reasonable to conclude that the total market value is less

than it would have been by at least:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>$100,000, if the total of the <sup>*</sup>adjustable values, immediately

before the <sup>*</sup>realisation event, of the <sup>*</sup>primary interests

referred to in subsection&#160;(2) is less than or equal to $2,000,000; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>5% of the total of those <sup>*</sup>adjustable values, if that total is

greater than $2,000,000 and less than or equal to $10,000,000; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>$500,000, if that total is greater than $10,000,000.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsections&#160;(2) and (3), disregard an

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift referred to in paragraph&#160;(2)(a) or (b) if

services are provided directly by the <sup>*</sup>losing entity to the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity under the <sup>*</sup>scheme before the income year

(of the losing entity) before the one in which the <sup>*</sup>realisation

event happened.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-715  Service arrangements reduce value of losing entity that is a group service provider by at least $500,000

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>At some time during the period (the _ownership period_) when

the owner owned the interest, the sole or dominant activity of the

<sup>*</sup>losing entity must consist of providing services directly to one or

more entities (the _group entities_) each of which is covered by

one or more of the following paragraphs:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an <sup>*</sup>affected owner;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an entity that has at that time the same <sup>*</sup>ultimate controller

as the losing entity or the gaining entity;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the conditions in section&#160;727-110 (common-ownership nexus test)

are satisfied for the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift&#151;an entity that has with

the losing entity or with the gaining entity a <sup>*</sup>common-ownership

nexus within that period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>It must be reasonable to conclude that the total (the _total market value_) of the market values, immediately before the

<sup>*</sup>realisation event, of <sup>*</sup>primary interests in the

<sup>*</sup>losing entity then owned by <sup>*</sup>affected owners is less

than it would have been if none of the following had happened:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>95% services indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each <sup>*</sup>predominantly-services indirect value shift for which the

same entity is the losing entity as for the 95% services indirect value shift,

and that happened:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the amount of the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift is $500,000 or

more&#151;at any time during the ownership period; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;during the ownership period but within 4 years before the

realisation event, or at the same time as the realisation event.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Thresholds for reduction of the total market value_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>It must also be reasonable to conclude that the total market value is less

than it would have been by at least $500,000, and by at least the lesser of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>5% of the total of the <sup>*</sup>adjustable values of

<sup>*</sup>primary interests in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity owned by

<sup>*</sup>affected owners at:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if subsection&#160;(4) applies&#151;the time determined under that subsection;

or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;the start of the income year in which the

<sup>*</sup>realisation event happens; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount worked out under the table.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the owner of the interest is an <sup>*</sup>affected owner because of

item&#160;1, 2, 3 or 4 in the table in subsection 727-530(1) (about who is an

affected owner), the time for the purposes of subparagraph&#160;(3)(a)(i) of

this section is the latest of:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the start of the income year in which the <sup>*</sup>realisation event

happens; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the most recent time (if any), before or at the time of the

<sup>*</sup>realisation event, when at least one of the group entities has the

same <sup>*</sup>ultimate controller as the losing entity or the gaining

entity; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the start of the most recent period (if any):

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>that ended before or at the time of the realisation event; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>within which at least one of the group entities has with the losing

entity or with the gaining entity a <sup>*</sup>common-ownership nexus.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

727-720  Abnormal service arrangement reduces value of losing entity that is not a group service provider by at least $500,000

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>It must be the case that at _no_ time during the period when the

owner owned the interest did the sole or dominant activity of the

<sup>*</sup>losing entity consist of providing services as mentioned in

subsection 727-715(1).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>It must be reasonable to conclude that the total (the _total market value_) of the market values, immediately before the <sup>*</sup>realisation event, of <sup>*</sup>primary interests in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity then owned by <sup>*</sup>affected owners is less than it would have been if none of the following had happened: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>95% services indirect value shift;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each <sup>*</sup>predominantly-services indirect value shift that meets

either of these conditions:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>its amount was less than $500,000 and it happened within 4 years before

the realisation event, or at the same time as the realisation event;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>its amount was $500,000 or more and it happened at any time before the

realisation event, or at the same time as the realisation event;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		and that meets all of these conditions:

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the same entity is the losing entity for it as for the 95% services

indirect value shift;</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>it happened under a different <sup>*</sup>scheme from the 95% services

indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(v)</dt><dd>having regard to all relevant circumstances, it is reasonable to conclude

that the sole or main reason why it happened under a different scheme was to

prevent the conditions in section&#160;727-705, 727-710, 727-715 or this

section from being met.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>It must also be reasonable to conclude that the total market value is less

than it would have been by at least:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>$500,000, if the total of the <sup>*</sup>adjustable values, immediately

before the <sup>*</sup>realisation event, of the <sup>*</sup>primary interests

referred to in subsection&#160;(2) is less than or equal to $10,000,000; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>5% of the total of those <sup>*</sup>adjustable values, if that total is

greater than $10,000,000 and less than or equal to $100,000,000; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>$5,000,000, if that total is greater than $100,000,000.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The providing of the services mentioned in paragraph 727-700(2)(a) or (b)

by the losing entity must _not_ be in the ordinary course of its business.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-725  Meaning of predominantly-services indirect value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		An <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift is a _predominantly-services indirect value shift_ if, and only if, the <sup>*</sup>greater benefits

consist entirely or predominantly of:

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a right to have services that are covered by section&#160;727-240 provided

directly by the <sup>*</sup>losing entity to the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>services that are covered by section&#160;727-240 and have been, are

being, or are to be, so provided;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

or both.

Subdivision&#160;727-H&#151;The adjustable value method
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;727-H
 727-750  What this Subdivision is about

Under the adjustable value method:

*	the adjustable values of affected interests in the losing entity are reduced; and

*	the adjustable values of affected interests in the gaining entity are uplifted, within limits worked out by references to the reductions in the adjustable values of affected interests in the losing entity.

The consequences of that are:

*	the cost base and reduced cost base of the interests are reduced or uplifted (or both); and

*	if the interests are also trading stock or revenue assets, there are further consequences for them in their character as such.

 727-840	Revenue assets

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

727-755  Consequences of indirect value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Subdivision sets out the _adjustable value method_ of

working out the consequences (if any) of an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If those consequences are to be worked out using that method: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of each <sup>*</sup>affected interest in

the <sup>*</sup>losing entity is reduced as provided in this Subdivision; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity is a company or trust (except one listed

in section&#160;727-125 (about superannuation entities)) immediately before the

<sup>*</sup>IVS time, the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of each

<sup>*</sup>affected interest in the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity is uplifted as

provided in this Subdivision.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The consequences for the <sup>*</sup>affected interest depend on its

character. There are consequences for the interest in its character as a

<sup>*</sup>CGT asset. However, if the interest is also <sup>*</sup>trading

stock or a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset, there are additional consequences for it

in that character.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 727-770.]_

Reductions of adjustable value
 727-770  Reduction under the adjustable value method

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section sets out how to work out the amount (if any) by which the

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value of an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the

<sup>*</sup>losing entity is reduced.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>First, work out under section&#160;727-775 whether the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift has produced for the owner of the interest a <sup>*</sup>disaggregated attributable decrease in the market value of the interest.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If it has not, the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is _not_ reduced because of the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>If it has, the amount (if any) by which the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is reduced is worked out on a <sup>*</sup>loss-focussed basis under section&#160;727-780.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>However, if a choice is made in accordance with section&#160;727-550 for the reduction _not_ to be worked out on a <sup>*</sup>loss-focussed basis, the reduction is equal to the <sup>*</sup>disaggregated attributable decrease. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Reduction not to exceed reasonable amount_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the reduction worked out as provided in subsection&#160;(4) or (5) is

not reasonable in the circumstances, having regard to the objects of this

Division, the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is instead reduced by so

much of that reduction as is reasonable in the circumstances, having regard to

those objects.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The main object of this Division is set out in

section&#160;727-95.

 </dl></dl>

727-775  Has there been a disaggregated attributable decrease?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section sets out how to determine whether an <sup>*</sup>indirect

value shift has produced, for the owner of an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan

interest, a _disaggregated attributable decrease_ in the market

value of the interest and, if so, the amount of it.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Work out the market value of the interest at the <sup>*</sup>IVS time, but disregarding: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>all effects on the market value of the interest during the <sup>*</sup>IVS

period, except effects that are reasonably attributable to the

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the effects (if any) of the indirect value shift on the market value of

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests, or <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan

interests, in the gaining entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

(This result is called the _notional resulting market value_.)

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph&#160;(2)(b) is necessary because the market value

of the interest may also have been affected by the increase in the market value

of interests in the gaining entity, because the entity in which the interest is

held had direct or indirect interests in both the losing entity and the gaining

entity. 	In such a case, the reduction in adjustable value under this Division will usually be offset by an uplift under this Division.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the notional resulting market value is _less than_ the market

value (the _old market value_) of the interest:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at the start of the <sup>*</sup>IVS period; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the owner last began to own the interest during that period&#151;when the

owner last began to own the interest;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the difference is the _disaggregated attributable decrease_.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift has _not_ produced a

disaggregated attributable decrease for the owner of the interest if the

notional resulting market value is _greater than or equal to_ the

old market value.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>The market value of the interest at a particular time may be worked out under subsection&#160;(2) or (3) by making a reasonable estimate of that market value. </dd> </dl></dl>

727-780  Working out the reduction on a loss-focussed basis

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Use the table in subsection&#160;(2) of this section to work out on a

_loss-focussed basis_ the amount (if any) by which the interest's

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value is reduced.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>This involves comparing the old market value, and the notional resulting market value, with the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value (the _old adjustable value_) immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time. </dd> </dl></dl>

    <div>is <i>less than</i>the old adjustable value</div>

  </td>

    <div>the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is reduced by the amount of the <sup>*</sup>disaggregated attributable decrease</div>

  </td>
