Note 1:	Because of item&#160;1, the indirect value shift cannot

cause a loss to arise on disposal of the interest. Note 2:	Because of item&#160;3 the loss already embedded in the interest is preserved, but the indirect value shift does not increase it.  </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 727-800.]_

Uplifts of adjustable value
 727-800  Uplift under the attributable increase method

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section sets out how to work out the amount (if any) by which the

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value of an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity is uplifted.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>First, work out under section&#160;727-805 whether the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift has produced for the owner of the interest a <sup>*</sup>disaggregated attributable increase in the market value of the interest.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If it has not, the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is _not_ uplifted because of the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>If it has, the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is uplifted by the amount worked out using the scaling-down formula in section&#160;727-810, subject to the rest of this section. </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The uplift will be less than or equal to the disaggregated

attributable increase.

 </dl></dl>

_Cap if interest has both a disaggregated attributable increase and a disaggregated attributable decrease_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift has also produced for the owner of

the interest a <sup>*</sup>disaggregated attributable decrease in the market

value of the interest, the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is _not_ uplifted if it is not also reduced under this Division

because of the indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if it is also reduced under this Division because of the indirect value

shift&#151;is not uplifted by more than the reduction.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Cap based on notional distribution by gaining entity of dividends or capital equal to total reductions in adjustable value of affected interests in losing entity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>However, the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is not uplifted by

more than the greater of these amounts:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) that the <sup>*</sup>affected owner of the interest

would receive (directly, or indirectly through one or more interposed entities)

in respect of the interest if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity were to pay as <sup>*</sup>dividends, at

the time (the _payment time_) immediately before the

<sup>*</sup>IVS time, an amount (the _total reduction amount_)

equal to the total of the amounts by which the <sup>*</sup>adjustable values of

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity are

reduced under this Subdivision because of the <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift;

and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>those dividends were successively paid or distributed at the payment time

by each entity interposed between the gaining entity and that affected owner;

and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount (if any) that the <sup>*</sup>affected owner of the interest

would receive (directly, or indirectly through one or more interposed entities)

in respect of the interest if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the gaining entity were to pay the total reduction amount at the payment

time as a distribution of capital; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>that capital was successively paid or distributed at the payment time by

each entity interposed between the gaining entity and that affected owner.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Uplift not to exceed reasonable amount_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>If the uplift worked out as provided in subsections&#160;(4), (5) and (6)

is not reasonable in the circumstances, having regard to the objects of this

Division, the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value is instead uplifted by an

amount that is reasonable in the circumstances, having regard to those objects.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The main object of this Division is set out in

section&#160;727-95.

 </dl></dl>

727-805  Has there been a disaggregated attributable increase?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section sets out how to determine whether an <sup>*</sup>indirect

value shift has produced, for the owner of an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan

interest, a _disaggregated attributable increase_ in the market

value of the interest and, if so, the amount of it.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Make a reasonable estimate of the market value of the interest at the <sup>*</sup>IVS time, but disregarding: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>all effects on the market value of the interest during the <sup>*</sup>IVS

period, except effects that are reasonably attributable to the

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the effects (if any) of the indirect value shift on the market value of

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests, or <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan

interests, in the losing entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

(This result is called the _notional resulting market value_.)

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph&#160;(2)(b) is necessary because the market value

of the interest may also have been affected by the decrease in the market value

of interests in the losing entity, because the entity in which the interest is

held had direct or indirect interests in both the losing entity and the gaining

entity. 	In such a case, the increase in adjustable value under this Division will usually be offset by a reduction under this Division.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the notional resulting market value is _greater than_ a reasonable

estimate of the market value (the _old market value_) of the

interest:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at the start of the <sup>*</sup>IVS period; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the owner last began to own the interest during that period&#151;when the

owner last began to own the interest;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the difference is the _disaggregated attributable increase_.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift has _not_ produced a

disaggregated attributable increase for the owner of the interest if the

notional resulting market value is _less than or equal to_ the old

market value.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-810  Scaling-down formula

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The scaling-down formula for the purposes of section&#160;727-800 is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1226.gif)</sub>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The numerator in the fraction can never exceed the

denominator. This means that the fraction can never exceed 1, so the uplift

will never exceed the disaggregated attributable increase.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of the formula:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_total disaggregated attributable decreases_ means the total of:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>all <sup>*</sup>disaggregated attributable decreases that the

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift has produced, in the market values of

<sup>*</sup>affected interests in the <sup>*</sup>losing entity, for the

entities that owned those interests immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS

time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-850 (as applying to the <sup>*</sup>scheme from which the

indirect value shift results) reduces losses that are <sup>*</sup>realised for

income tax purposes by <sup>*</sup>realisation events happening before the

<sup>*</sup>IVS time to <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests, or to

<sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interests, in the losing entity; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the indirect value shift is the only indirect value shift, or is the

greater or greatest of 2 or more indirect value shifts, that results from the

scheme and for which the losing entity is the losing entity;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		for each of those realisation events, the amounts that would, if:

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>presumed indirect value shift were an indirect value

shift; and</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>the IVS time for the presumed indirect value shift were the time of that

realisation event;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		be the disaggregated attributable decreases that the presumed indirect value

shift has produced, in the market value of the equity or loan interests to

which that realisation event happened, for the entities that owned those

interests immediately before the time of that realisation event.

</dl></dl></dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_total reductions for affected interests_ means the total of:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>all reductions under this Division, because of the indirect value shift,

of <sup>*</sup>adjustable values of affected interests in the losing entity;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if paragraph&#160;(b) of the definition of _total disaggregated attributable decreases_ applies&#151;the amounts by which

section&#160;727-850 reduces the losses (if any) referred to in that paragraph.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 727-830.]_

Consequences of the method for various kinds of assets
 727-830  CGT assets

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>cost base of an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest is

reduced or uplifted immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time to the extent

that this Division provides for the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the

interest to be reduced or uplifted.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest is reduced or uplifted immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time to the extent that this Division provides for the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the interest to be reduced or uplifted.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>However, the <sup>*</sup>cost base or <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base is _uplifted_ only to the extent that the amount of the uplift is still reflected in the market value of the interest when a later <sup>*</sup>CGT event happens to the interest.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>To work out: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>whether the <sup>*</sup>cost base or <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of the

interest is reduced or uplifted; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if so, by how much;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

assume that the _adjustable value_ from time to time of that or any other <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest is its cost base or reduced cost base, as appropriate.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If this Division provides for the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of an

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest to be _both_ reduced and uplifted:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the reduction and uplift for which subsection&#160;(1) or (2) of this

section provides offset each other to the extent of whichever of them is the

lesser; but</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if subsection&#160;(3) of this section cancels or reduces the uplift, this

subsection is taken always to have applied on that basis.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Reductions and uplifts also apply to pre-CGT assets_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A reduction or uplift occurs regardless of whether the entity that owns

the interest <sup>*</sup>acquired it before, on or after 20&#160;September 1985.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-835  Trading stock

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section deals with:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>how this Division applies to an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest that

is <sup>*</sup>trading stock of an entity at the time (the _adjustment time_) immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the income tax consequences of this Division reducing or uplifting the

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The interest's _adjustable value_ at a particular time is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the interest has been <sup>*</sup>trading stock of the entity ever

since the start of the income year of the entity in which that time occurs&#151;its

<sup>*</sup>value as trading stock at the start of the income year; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;its cost.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If this Division reduces or uplifts the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable

value, the entity is treated as if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>immediately before the adjustment time, the entity had sold the interest

to someone else (at <sup>*</sup>arm's length and in the ordinary course of

business) for its <sup>*</sup>adjustable value immediately before that time;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>immediately after the adjustment time, the entity had bought the interest

back for the reduced or uplifted adjustable value.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The notional sale and repurchase are separated in time. As

a result, if this section is applied to another indirect value shift that

happens later in the same income year, the interest's adjustable value will be

the cost on the notional repurchase: see paragraph&#160;(2)(b).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, the increase in the cost of an interest because of

paragraph&#160;(3)(b) is taken into account from time to time only to the

extent that the amount of the increase is still reflected in the market value

of the interest.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The situations where the increase in cost would be taken

into account include:

 </dl></dl>

*	in working out your deductions for the cost of trading stock acquired during the income year in which the increase happens; and
 *	the end of an income year if the interest's closing value as trading stock is worked out on the basis of its cost; and
 *	the start of the income year in which the interest is disposed of, if that happens in a later income year and the interest's closing value as trading stock at the end of the previous income year was worked out on the basis of its cost.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If this Division provides for the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the

interest to be _both_ reduced and uplifted:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the reduction and uplift offset each other to the extent of whichever of

them is the lesser, and subsection&#160;(3) of this section applies

accordingly; but</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to the extent that the amount of the uplift is no longer reflected in the

market value of the interest, this section is taken always to have applied on

the basis that the amount of the uplift was reduced to the same extent.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

727-840  Revenue assets

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This section deals with:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>how this Division applies to an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest that

is a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset of an entity at the time (the _adjustment time_) immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the income tax consequences of this Division reducing or uplifting the

<sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The interest's _adjustable value_ at a particular time is the

total of the amounts that would be subtracted from the gross disposal proceeds

in calculating any profit or loss on disposal of the interest if the entity

disposed of it at that time.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If this Division reduces or uplifts the interest's <sup>*</sup>adjustable value, the entity is treated as if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>immediately before the adjustment time, the entity had sold the interest

to someone else (at <sup>*</sup>arm's length and in the ordinary course of

business) for its adjustable value immediately before that time; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>immediately after the adjustment time, the entity had bought the interest

back for the reduced or uplifted adjustable value.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The notional sale and repurchase are separated in time. As

a result, if this section is applied to another indirect value shift that

happens later in the same income year, the interest's adjustable value will be

based on the cost on the notional repurchase: see subsection&#160;(2).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>However, an uplift in the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the interest is

taken into account only to the extent that the amount of the uplift is still

reflected in the market value of the interest when it is disposed of or

otherwise realised.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If this Division provides for the <sup>*</sup>adjustable value of the interest to be _both_ reduced and uplifted: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the reduction and uplift offset each other to the extent of whichever of

them is the lesser, and subsection&#160;(3) of this section applies

accordingly; but</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>to the extent that the amount of the uplift is no longer reflected in the

market value of the interest, this section is taken always to have applied on

the basis that the amount of the uplift was reduced to the same extent.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;727-K&#151;Reduction of loss on equity or loan interests realised before the IVS time 

Table of sections

727-850	Consequences of scheme under this Subdivision
 727-855	Presumed indirect value shift
 727-860	Conditions about the prospective gaining entity
 727-865	How other provisions of this Division apply to support this Subdivision
 727-870	Effect of CGT roll-over
 727-875	Application to CGT asset that is also trading stock or revenue asset

727-850  Consequences of scheme under this Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>as at the time when a <sup>*</sup>scheme is entered into, or a later time,

an entity (the _prospective losing entity_) has

<sup>*</sup>provided, is providing, is to provide, or might provide, one or

more economic benefits <sup>*</sup>in connection with the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the prospective losing entity is a company or trust (except one listed in

section&#160;727-125 (about superannuation entities)); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>realisation event happens to an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan

interest, or to an <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interest, in the

prospective losing entity at a time when no <sup>*</sup>IVS time for the scheme

has yet happened (whether or not one happens later); and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>apart from this Division, a loss would be <sup>*</sup>realised for income

tax purposes by the realisation event; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>because of section&#160;727-855, the scheme results in a

<sup>*</sup>presumed indirect value shift affecting the realisation event;

and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-860 (about prospective gaining entities) is satisfied;

and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>no exclusion in Subdivision&#160;727-C applies to the presumed indirect

value shift because of section&#160;727-865; and</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>on the assumptions set out in subsection 727-865(3), the interest would be

an <sup>*</sup>affected interest in the prospective losing entity;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

the loss is reduced by an amount that is reasonable having regard to a reasonable estimate of the amount (if any) by which the scheme has reduced the interest's market value during the period that ends at the time of the realisation event and started at the later of:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>when the scheme was entered into; and</dd>

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>the time of the last realisation event that happened to the interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	This Subdivision does not reduce gains from realisation

events, but loss reductions under this Subdivision are taken into account in

working out:

 </dl></dl>

*	gain reductions under Subdivision&#160;727-G for interests in a gaining entity that are realised after the IVS time for the scheme (see section&#160;727-625); or
 *	uplifts under Subdivision&#160;727-H in the adjustable values of interests in a gaining entity (see section&#160;727-810).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 2:	Section&#160;727-865 provides for how other provisions of

this Division apply for the purposes of this Subdivision.

 </dl></dl>

_Further exclusion for certain 95% services indirect value shifts_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The loss is not reduced if the <sup>*</sup>presumed indirect value shift

is a <sup>*</sup>95% services indirect value shift because of subsection

727-865(2), unless:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the conditions in section&#160;727-705 (as applying because of that

subsection) are met for the presumed indirect value shift; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the conditions in section&#160;727-710, 727-715 or 727-720 (as applying

because of that subsection) are met for the presumed indirect value shift and

for the realisation event.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-855  Presumed indirect value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>scheme results in a _presumed indirect value shift_ affecting the <sup>*</sup>realisation event if, and only if, as

at the time of the realisation event, it is reasonable to conclude that the

total market value of the economic benefits (the _greater benefits_) that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>prospective losing entity has <sup>*</sup>provided, is

providing, is to provide, or might provide, <sup>*</sup>in connection with the

<sup>*</sup>scheme, to another entity, or to each of 2 or more other entities;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>can be identified (even if the other entity or entities cannot be

identified or are not all in existence, or the provision of some or all of the

economic benefits is contingent);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

exceeds:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the total market value of the economic benefits (the _lesser benefits_) that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>have been, are being, are to be, or might be, provided _to_ the

prospective losing entity in connection with the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>can be identified (even if the entity or entities providing the benefits

cannot be identified or are not all in existence, or the provision of some or

all of the economic benefits is contingent); or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if there are no economic benefits covered by paragraph&#160;(c)&#151;nil.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

That excess is the amount of the presumed indirect value shift, which happens at the time of the realisation event.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The market value of an economic benefit is to be determined as at the

earliest time when it is reasonable to conclude that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the economic benefit can be identified; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>paragraph 727-150(2)(b) is satisfied for that benefit;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

if that time is before the <sup>*</sup>realisation event.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Otherwise, the market value of the economic benefit is to be determined as

at the time immediately before the <sup>*</sup>realisation event, taking

account of any contingency to which provision of the benefit is subject at that

time.

</dd> </dl></dl>

For more rules affecting how the market value of an economic benefit is determined, see Subdivision&#160;727-D (as applying because of
subsection 727-865(1)).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>An entity referred to in paragraph&#160;(1)(a) need not be a party to the

<sup>*</sup>scheme. A benefit can be provided by act or omission.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-860  Conditions about the prospective gaining entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>By the deadline set out in subsection&#160;(5), the conditions in

subsections&#160;(2) and (3) must be satisfied for at least one of these

entities:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity or entities referred to in paragraph 727-855(1)(a);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if at the time of the <sup>*</sup>realisation event it is reasonable to

conclude that the entity, or at least one of the entities, referred to in

paragraph 727-855(1)(a) will be one of 2 or more entities, but it cannot be

determined which&#151;those 2 or more entities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Enough must be known about the identity of an entity covered by

subsection&#160;(1) for it to be reasonable to conclude that, if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>presumed indirect value shift were an <sup>*</sup>indirect

value shift resulting from the <sup>*</sup>scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>IVS period for the scheme ended at the time of the

<sup>*</sup>realisation event; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>that entity were the <sup>*</sup>gaining entity for the indirect value

shift;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>prospective losing entity were the <sup>*</sup>losing

entity for the indirect value shift; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

either or both of these would be satisfied for the indirect value shift:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-105 (Ultimate controller test); and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-110 (Common-ownership nexus test).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Enough must be known about the identity of the entity referred to in

subsection&#160;(2) for it also to be reasonable to conclude that, in relation

to either or both of the following:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>prospective losing entity <sup>*</sup>providing one or

more economic benefits to that entity <sup>*</sup>in connection with the

<sup>*</sup>scheme; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that entity providing one or more economic benefits to the prospective

losing entity in connection with the scheme;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

that entity and the prospective losing entity were not, are not, will not be, or would not be, dealing with each other at <sup>*</sup>arm's length.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Each entity that is covered by subsection&#160;(1), and for which

subsections&#160;(2) and (3) are satisfied, is called a _prospective gaining entity_ for the <sup>*</sup>scheme.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>The deadline is: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the entity that owned the <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest

immediately before the <sup>*</sup>realisation event must lodge an

<sup>*</sup>income tax return for the income year in which the event

happens&#151;the time by which the return must be lodged; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;the end of the 6 months immediately after that income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

727-865  How other provisions of this Division apply to support this Subdivision

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>To avoid doubt, these provisions apply for the purposes of working out

whether there has been a <sup>*</sup>presumed indirect value shift and, if so,

the amount of it:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>sections&#160;727-155, 727-160 and 727-165 (about economic benefits);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-315 (Transfer, for its adjustable value, of depreciating

asset acquired for less than $1,500,000).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of section&#160;727-850, these provisions:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>Subdivision&#160;727-C (Exclusions), except section&#160;727-260 (about a

shift down a wholly-owned chain of entities);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>sections&#160;727-700 to 727-725 (about 95% services indirect value

shifts), except subsection 727-700(1);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

apply to the <sup>*</sup>presumed indirect value shift on the assumptions set out in subsection&#160;(3).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The assumptions are:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>presumed indirect value shift is an <sup>*</sup>indirect

value shift resulting from the <sup>*</sup>scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>prospective losing entity for the scheme is the

<sup>*</sup>losing entity for that indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>each <sup>*</sup>prospective gaining entity for the scheme is the

<sup>*</sup>gaining entity for that indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>greater benefits under the presumed indirect value shift

are the greater benefits under that indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>lesser benefits (if any) under the presumed indirect value

shift are the lesser benefits under that indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the time of the realisation event mentioned in paragraph 727-850(1)(c) is

the <sup>*</sup>IVS time for the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>IVS period for the scheme ends at the time of the

realisation event; and</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-105 (Ultimate controller test) is satisfied for that

indirect value shift according to what it is reasonable to conclude under

subsection 727-860(2) as applying to the presumed indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-110 (Common-ownership nexus test) is satisfied for that

indirect value shift according to what it is reasonable to conclude under

subsection 727-860(2) as applying to the presumed indirect value shift; and</dd>

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>a reference to the realisation event mentioned in subsection 727-700(1)

were a reference to the realisation event mentioned in paragraph 727-850(1)(c);

and</dd>

<dt>(k)</dt><dd>the interest to which the realisation event mentioned in paragraph

727-850(1)(c) happens were the interest referred to in paragraph 727-700(1)(a);

and</dd>

<dt>(l)</dt><dd>a reference in any of sections&#160;727-700 to 727-725 (about 95% services

indirect value shifts), except subsection 727-700(1), to the owner were a

reference to the entity that, at the time of the realisation event mentioned in

paragraph 727-850(1)(c), owns the interest to which the event happens.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Sections&#160;727-635 and 727-640 affect how this Subdivision applies to

<sup>*</sup>equity or loan interests, and <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan

interests, in the <sup>*</sup>prospective losing entity that are split or

merged during the period:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>starting when the <sup>*</sup>scheme is entered into; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ending at the time of the <sup>*</sup>realisation event mentioned in

paragraph 727-850(1)(c);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

in the same way as those sections affect how Subdivision&#160;727-G would apply to those interests on the assumptions set out in subsection&#160;(3) of this section.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The application of a provision because of this section is additional to,

and is not intended to limit, any other application of the provision.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-870  Effect of CGT roll-over

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>realisation event mentioned in paragraph 727-850(1)(c) is

a <sup>*</sup>CGT event; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;727-850 reduces a loss that would, apart from this Division,

be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the CGT event; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>there is a roll-over for the CGT event;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the interest's <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base at the time of the CGT event is taken to have been reduced by the amount by which section&#160;727-850 reduces that loss, but is so taken only for the purposes of working out:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the interest's reduced cost base, from time to time after the roll-over,

for the entity that <sup>*</sup>acquired the interest because of the CGT event;

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>in the case of a <sup>*</sup>replacement-asset roll-over&#151;the reduced cost

base of the replacement CGT asset, from time to time after the roll-over, for

the entity that <sup>*</sup>disposed of the interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Because of the roll-over, the loss reduction under

section&#160;727-850 will have no tax effect. This subsection ensures that the

loss reduction is passed on, through the reduction in reduced cost base, to

prevent or reduce a loss arising on a later CGT event.

 </dl></dl>

727-875  Application to CGT asset that is also trading stock or revenue asset

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If an <sup>*</sup>equity or loan interest is also an item of

<sup>*</sup>trading stock or a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset, this Subdivision

applies to the interest once in its character as a CGT asset and again in its

character as trading stock or a revenue asset.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;727-L&#151;Indirect value shift resulting from a direct value shift 

Table of sections

727-905	How this Subdivision affects the rest of this Division
 727-910	Treatment of value shifted under the direct value shift

727-905  How this Subdivision affects the rest of this Division

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Subdivision affects how the rest of this Division applies to a

<sup>*</sup>scheme (the _IVS scheme_) that is or includes a scheme

(the _DVS scheme_) under which there is a <sup>*</sup>direct value

shift.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>has consequences under Division&#160;725 for an entity as an

<sup>*</sup>affected owner of <sup>*</sup>down interests (or would do so apart

from section&#160;725-90 (about direct value shifts that will be reversed));

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>also has consequences under that Division for another entity as an

affected owner of <sup>*</sup>up interests (or would do so apart from

section&#160;725-90);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the rest of this Subdivision has effect, for the purposes of Subdivisions&#160;727-A to 727-K, in order to determine:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>whether the IVS scheme results in an <sup>*</sup>indirect value shift,

from the first entity to the other entity, that has consequences under this

Division; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>whether the IVS scheme has consequences under Subdivision&#160;727-K

because it results in a <sup>*</sup>presumed indirect value shift affecting a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event happening to <sup>*</sup>equity or loan

interests, or to <sup>*</sup>indirect equity or loan interests, in the first

entity; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>those consequences.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;725-50 sets out when a direct value shift has

consequences under Division&#160;725.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the IVS scheme is the DVS scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>subsection 725-145(2) is satisfied for the <sup>*</sup>direct value shift

(because one or more equity or loan interests in the target entity are issued

at a discount); but</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>subsection 725-145(3) (about an increase in the market value of one or

more equity or loan interests in the target entity) is not satisfied for the

direct value shift;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivisions&#160;727-A to 727-K apply to the IVS scheme only as provided in this section.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Otherwise, those Subdivisions apply to the IVS scheme as provided in this

section in addition to any other application they have to the scheme.

</dd> </dl></dl>

727-910  Treatment of value shifted under the direct value shift

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The first entity is treated as <sup>*</sup>providing economic benefits to

the other entity, <sup>*</sup>in connection with the IVS scheme, at the time of

a decrease (or future decrease) in the market value of any of the

<sup>*</sup>down interests, to the extent that the decrease is (or will be)

covered by subsection 725-155(1).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Despite subsections 727-150(4) and 727-855(2) and (3), the market value of all economic benefits that subsection&#160;(1) of this section treats the first entity as providing to the other entity: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is to be determined as at the time immediately before the <sup>*</sup>IVS

time, or immediately before the <sup>*</sup>realisation event, as appropriate;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is equal to the total value shifted from the <sup>*</sup>down interests to

the <sup>*</sup>up interests, as worked out under one or more applications of

step 2 of the method statement in section&#160;725-365 or 725-380.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The 2 entities are treated as not dealing with each other at

<sup>*</sup>arm's length in relation to the providing of those benefits.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>None of those benefits is treated as consisting of, or including, services provided or a right to have services provided. </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This means that the exclusions in Subdivisions&#160;727-C

and 727-G for indirect value shifts involving services will not apply.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>Except as provided in this section, none of the following is treated as

the <sup>*</sup>providing of economic benefits <sup>*</sup>in connection with

the IVS scheme:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a decrease (or future decrease) in the market value of <sup>*</sup>down

interests owned by the first entity or the other entity, to the extent that the

decrease is (or will be) covered by subsection 725-155(1);</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an increase (or future increase) in the market value of <sup>*</sup>up

interests owned by the first entity or the other entity, to the extent that the

increase is (or will be) covered by subsection 725-145(3);</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an issue of <sup>*</sup>up interests at a <sup>*</sup>discount to the

first entity or the other entity, to the extent that the issue is (or will be)

covered by subsection 725-145(2).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Value shifted from down interests owned by the other entity

to up interests owned by the first entity are dealt with by a separate

application of this Subdivision to those interests (because of paragraphs

727-905(2)(a) and (b).

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Division&#160;725&#151;Direct value shifting affecting interests in companies and trusts

725-1  Application of Division&#160;725

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Division&#160;725 applies to a scheme entered into on or after 1&#160;July

2002\. It also applies to a scheme entered into on or after 27&#160;June 2002,

but only if:

 </dl></dl>

owners are all on or after 1&#160;July 2002; and</dd>

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Division&#160;727&#151;Indirect value shifting affecting interests in companies and trusts, and arising from non-arm's length dealings

727-1  Application of Division&#160;727

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Division&#160;727 applies to a scheme entered into on or after 1&#160;July

2002.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>It also applies to a scheme entered into on or after 27&#160;June 2002, but only in relation to: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an indirect value shift that happens under the scheme on or after

1&#160;July 2002; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a presumed indirect value shift that happens under the scheme and affects

a realisation event that happens on or after 1&#160;July 2002.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

presumed indirect value shift, if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the economic benefits taken into account in determining that the scheme

has resulted in that indirect value shift or presumed indirect value shift

include economic benefits provided by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an act referred to in Division&#160;138 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ as the trigger event; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an event or act referred to in Division&#160;139 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ as the trigger event; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the act was done, or the event happened, on or after 27&#160;June 2002 and

before 1&#160;July 2002.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	In that case, the consequences of the trigger event are

worked out under Division&#160;138 or 139 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_: see items&#160;13 and 14 of Schedule&#160;15 to the _New Business Tax System (Consolidation, Value Shifting, Demergers and Other Measures) Act 2002_.

 </dl></dl>

Division&#160;2&#151;Saving and transitional provisions
 13  Saving for former Division&#160;138

Despite the repeal by item&#160;9, the repealed provisions continue to apply to an act referred to in Division&#160;138 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ as the trigger event, if the act was done:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>under a scheme entered into before 27&#160;June 2002; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on or after 27&#160;June 2002 and before 1&#160;July 2002.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

14  Saving for former Division&#160;139

Despite the repeal by item&#160;10, the repealed provisions continue to apply to an event or act referred to in Division&#160;139 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ as the trigger event, if the event happened, or the act was done:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>under a scheme entered into before 27&#160;June 2002; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on or after 27&#160;June 2002 and before 1&#160;July 2002.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

15  Saving for former provisions about direct value shifts

Despite the repeal by item&#160;11, the repealed provisions continue to apply to a scheme, unless Division&#160;725 of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_ applies to the scheme.

Part&#160;5&#151;Dictionary amendments

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

19  After Division&#160;975

Insert:

Division&#160;977&#151;Realisation events, and the gains and losses they realise for income tax purposes

Table of sections

CGT assets

977-5	Realisation event
 977-10	Loss realised for income tax purposes
 977-15	Gain realised for income tax purposes

Trading stock

977-20	Realisation event
 977-25	Disposal of trading stock: loss realised for income tax purposes
 977-30	Ending of an income year: loss realised for income tax purposes
 977-35	Disposal of trading stock: gain realised for income tax purposes
 977-40	Ending of an income year: gain realised for income tax purposes

Revenue assets

977-50	Meaning of _revenue asset_

 977-55	Loss or gain realised for income tax purposes

CGT assets
 977-5  Realisation event

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		For a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset, a _realisation event_ is a

<sup>*</sup>CGT event (except CGT event E4 and CGT event G1).

 </dl></dl>

977-10  Loss realised for income tax purposes

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A loss is _realised for income tax purposes_<sup> </sup>by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset if, and

only if, an entity makes a <sup>*</sup>capital loss from the event. That

capital loss is the loss realised by the event.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a provision of this Act reduces the loss that would, apart from that provision, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the event, the <sup>*</sup>capital loss is reduced by the same amount. </dd> </dl></dl>

977-15  Gain realised for income tax purposes

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A gain is _realised for income tax purposes_<sup> </sup>by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset if, and

only if, an entity makes a <sup>*</sup>capital gain from the event. That

capital gain is the gain that is realised by the event.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a provision of this Act reduces the gain that would, apart from that provision, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the event, the <sup>*</sup>capital gain is reduced by the same amount. </dd> </dl></dl>

Trading stock
 977-20  Realisation event

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		For an item of <sup>*</sup>trading stock, a _realisation event_

is a disposal of the item or the ending of an income year.

 </dl></dl>

977-25  Disposal of trading stock: loss realised for income tax purposes

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A loss is _realised for income tax purposes_<sup> </sup>by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event consisting of disposal of an item of

<sup>*</sup>trading stock if, and only if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the item is disposed of, for less than its <sup>*</sup>cost, in the same

income year in which it became part of the trading stock on hand of the entity

disposing of it; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item is disposed of in a later income year for less than its

<sup>*</sup>value as trading stock of the entity on hand at the start of the

later income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The loss that is realised for income tax purposes by the event is the

difference between the amount included in the entity's assessable income

because of the disposal and:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount that the entity can deduct for the item's <sup>*</sup>cost;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item's <sup>*</sup>value as <sup>*</sup>trading stock on hand at the

start of the later income year;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as appropriate.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a provision of this Act reduces the loss that would, apart from that

provision, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the event:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount that the entity can deduct for the item's <sup>*</sup>cost;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item's <sup>*</sup>value as trading stock on hand at the start of the

later income year;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as appropriate, is reduced by the same amount.

977-30  Ending of an income year: loss realised for income tax purposes

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A loss is _realised for income tax purposes_<sup> </sup>by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to an item of <sup>*</sup>trading

stock  and consists of the ending of an income year if, and only

if, the <sup>*</sup>value of the item, as trading stock of an entity on hand at

the end of that income year, is less than:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>its <sup>*</sup>cost, if it became part of the trading stock on hand of

the entity during that income year; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise, its value as trading stock of the entity on hand at the start

of that income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The loss that is realised for income tax purposes by the event is the

difference between the <sup>*</sup>value of the item, as <sup>*</sup>trading

stock of the entity on hand at the end of that income year and:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount that the entity can deduct for the item's <sup>*</sup>cost;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item's <sup>*</sup>value as trading stock on hand at the start of the

income year;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as appropriate.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a provision of this Act reduces the loss that would, apart from that

provision, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the event:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount that the entity can deduct for the item's <sup>*</sup>cost;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item's <sup>*</sup>value as <sup>*</sup>trading stock on hand at the

start of the income year;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as appropriate, is reduced by the same amount.

977-35  Disposal of trading stock: gain realised for income tax purposes

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A gain is _realised for income tax purposes_ by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event consisting of disposal of an item of

<sup>*</sup>trading stock if, and only if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the item is disposed of, for more than its <sup>*</sup>cost, in the same

income year in which it became part of the trading stock on hand of the entity

disposing of it; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item is disposed of in a later income year for more than its

<sup>*</sup>value as trading stock of the entity on hand at the start of the

later income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The gain that is realised for income tax purposes by the event is the

difference between the amount included in the entity's assessable income

because of the disposal and:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount that the entity can deduct for the item's <sup>*</sup>cost;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item's <sup>*</sup>value as trading stock on hand at the start of the

later income year;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as appropriate.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a provision of this Act reduces the gain that would, apart from that

provision, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the event, the

amount that is included in the assessable income of the entity because of the

disposal is reduced by the same amount.

</dd> </dl></dl>

977-40  Ending of an income year: gain realised for income tax purposes

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A gain is _realised for income tax purposes_ by a

<sup>*</sup>realisation event that happens to an item of <sup>*</sup>trading

stock  and consists of the ending of an income year if, and only

if, the <sup>*</sup>value of the item, as trading stock of an entity on hand at

the end of that income year, is greater than:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>its <sup>*</sup>cost, if it became part of the trading stock on hand of

the entity during that income year; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise, its value as trading stock of the entity on hand at the start

of that income year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The gain that is realised for income tax purposes by the event is the

difference between the <sup>*</sup>value of the item, as <sup>*</sup>trading

stock of the entity on hand at the end of that income year and:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount that the entity can deduct for the item's <sup>*</sup>cost;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item's <sup>*</sup>value as trading stock on hand at the start of the

income year;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as appropriate.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a provision of this Act reduces the gain that would, apart from that

provision, be <sup>*</sup>realised for income tax purposes by the event:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount that the entity can deduct for the item's <sup>*</sup>cost;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the item's <sup>*</sup>value as <sup>*</sup>trading stock on hand at the

start of the income year;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

as appropriate, is increased by the same amount.

_\[The next section is sectionÂ 977-50.]_

Revenue assets 
 977-50  Meaning of revenue asset

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>CGT asset is a _revenue asset_ if, and only if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the profit or loss on your disposing of the asset, ceasing to own it, or

otherwise realising it, would be taken into account, in calculating your

assessable income or <sup>*</sup>tax loss, otherwise than as a

<sup>*</sup>capital gain or <sup>*</sup>capital loss; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the asset is neither <sup>*</sup>trading stock nor a

<sup>*</sup>depreciating asset.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

 977-55  Loss or gain realised for income tax purposes

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		For a <sup>*</sup>revenue asset:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>disposing of, ceasing to own, or otherwise realising, the asset is a

_realisation event_; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a loss is _realised for income tax purposes_<sup> </sup>by the

<sup>*</sup>realisation event if, and only if, there is a loss on the event;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a gain is _realised for income tax purposes_<sup> </sup>by the

realisation event if, and only if, there is a profit on the event; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the loss or profit on the event is the loss or gain realised for income

tax purposes; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>if a provision of this Act reduces the loss or gain that would, apart from

that provision, be realised for income tax purposes by the event, the loss or

profit to be taken into account in calculating your assessable income or

<sup>*</sup>tax loss is reduced by the same amount.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

value shift&#151;has the meaning given by sections&#160;725-240, 725-315 and

725-325; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>for the purposes of determining the consequences of an

<sup>*</sup>indirect value shift&#151;has the meaning given by

</dd>
