87  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_ultimate stake_ of a particular percentage has the meaning given

by sections&#160;727-405, 727-410 and 727-415.

 </dl></dl>

88  Subsection 995-1(1) (definition of under common ownership)

Repeal the definition, substitute:

<center>Back to Top</center>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_under common ownership_: 2 companies are _under common ownership_ if, and only if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>they are members of the same <sup>*</sup>wholly-owned group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>after tracing the direct and indirect ownership of the <sup>*</sup>shares

in each of the companies (through any interposed companies and trusts) to the

individuals who ultimately hold it, that ownership is held by the same

individuals in the same proportions.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

In doing the tracing, ignore <sup>*</sup>shares whose <sup>*</sup>dividends can reasonably be regarded as being equivalent to the payment of interest on a loan having regard to:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>how the dividends are calculated; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the conditions applying to the payment of the dividends; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>any other relevant matters.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

89  Subsection 995-1(1)

Insert:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_up interest_ has the meaning given by section&#160;725-155.

 </dl></dl>

<center>**

###  NEW BUSINESS TAX SYSTEM (CONSOLIDATION, VALUE SHIFTING, DEMERGERS AND OTHER MEASURES) ACT 2002Schedule&#160;16&#151;Demerger relief 
**</center>

 Part&#160;1&#151;CGT relief 

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_

1  After Division&#160;124

Insert:

Division&#160;125&#151;Demerger relief

Table of Subdivisions

	Guide to Division&#160;125
 125-A	Object of this Division
 125-B	Consequences for owners of interests
 125-C	Consequences for members of demerger group
 125-D	Corporate unit trusts and public trading trusts

Guide to Division&#160;125
 125-1  What this Division is about

Entities can obtain CGT relief for a demerger.
 Owners of ownership interests in the head entity of a demerger group can obtain a roll-over to defer CGT consequences for the CGT events that happen to their interests under the demerger (see Subdivision&#160;125-B).
 Capital gains and capital losses made by members of the demerger group from certain CGT events that happen under the demerger are disregarded (see Subdivision&#160;125-C).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Dividend relief is also available: see section&#160;44 of

the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;125-A&#151;Object of this Division

Table of sections

125-5	Object of this Division

125-5  Object of this Division

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		The object of this Division is to facilitate the demerging of entities by

ensuring that capital gains tax considerations are not an impediment to

restructuring a <sup>*</sup>business.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;125-B&#151;Consequences for owners of interests
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;125-B
 125-50  Guide to Subdivision&#160;125-B

You can choose to obtain a roll-over if a CGT event happens to your interests in a company or trust because of a demerger of an entity from the group of which the company or trust is the head entity.
 There are cost base adjustments if you receive new interests under a demerger and no CGT event happens to your original interests.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

<center>Back to Top</center>

125-55	When a roll-over is available for a demerger
 125-60	Meaning of _ownership interest_ and related terms
 125-65	Meanings of _demerger group_, _head entity_ and _demerger subsidiary_
 125-70	Meanings of _demerger_, _demerged entity_ and _demerging entity_
 125-75	Exception: employee share schemes
 125-80	What is the roll-over?
 125-85	Cost base adjustments where CGT event happens but no roll-over chosen
 125-90	Cost base adjustments where no CGT event
 125-95	No other cost base adjustment after demerger
 125-100	No further demerger relief in some cases

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 125-55  When a roll-over is available for a demerger

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>You can choose to obtain a roll-over if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>you own an <sup>*</sup>ownership interest in a company or trust (your

_original interest_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company or trust is the <sup>*</sup>head entity of a

<sup>*</sup>demerger group; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>demerger happens to the demerger group; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>under the demerger, a <sup>*</sup>CGT event happens to your original

interest and you <sup>*</sup>acquire a new or replacement interest (your

_new interest_) in the <sup>*</sup>demerged entity.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section&#160;125-80 sets out what the roll-over is. Note 2:	You have to make cost base adjustments even if there is no CGT event: see section&#160;125-90\. Example:	Peter owns shares (his original interests) in Company A, a public company. Company B is a wholly owned subsidiary of Company A. Company A announces a demerger utilising a proportionate capital reduction and the disposal of all its shares in Company B to its 320,000 shareholders. Following the demerger all of the shareholders in Company A, including Peter, will own all of the shares in Company B (their new interests).  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>You cannot choose to obtain a roll-over under this Subdivision for an

original interest if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>you are a foreign resident; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the new interest you <sup>*</sup>acquire under the <sup>*</sup>demerger in

exchange for that original interest does not have the <sup>*</sup>necessary

connection with Australia just after you acquire it.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section&#160;136-25 tells you when an asset has the

necessary connection with Australia.

 </dl></dl>

125-60  Meaning of ownership interest and related terms

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An _ownership interest_ in a company or trust is:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>for a company, a <sup>*</sup>share in the company or an option, right or

similar interest issued by the company that gives the owner an entitlement to

<sup>*</sup>acquire a share in the company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for a trust, a unit or other interest in the trust or an option, right or

similar interest issued by the trustee that gives the owner an entitlement to

acquire a unit or other interest in the trust.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>However, this Subdivision applies to a <sup>*</sup>dual listed company

voting share in a company as if it were not an _ownership interest_

if there are not more than 5 of those <sup>*</sup>shares in the company.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A _dual listed company voting share_ is a <sup>*</sup>share in a company: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>issued:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>in the <sup>*</sup>head entity of a <sup>*</sup>demerger group; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>as part of a <sup>*</sup>dual listed company arrangement; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>mainly for the purpose of ensuring that shareholders of both companies

involved in the arrangement vote as a single decision-making body on matters

affecting them; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that does not carry rights to financial entitlements (except the return of

the amount paid up on the share and a dividend that is the equivalent of a

dividend paid on an ordinary share).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A _dual listed company arrangement_ is an

<sup>*</sup>arrangement under which 2 publicly listed companies, while

maintaining their separate legal entity status, shareholdings and listings,

align their strategic directions and the economic interests of their respective

shareholders through:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the appointment of common (or almost identical) boards of directors; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>management of the operations of the 2 companies on a unified basis; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the shareholders of both companies voting in effect as a single

decision-making body on substantial issues affecting their combined interests;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>equalised distributions to shareholders in accordance with an equalisation

ratio applying between the 2 companies, both generally and in the event of a

winding up of one or both of the companies; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>cross-guarantees as to, or similar financial support for, each other's

substantial obligations or operations, except where the effect of the relevant

regulatory requirements prevents those guarantees or that financial support.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>However, an arrangement is not a _dual listed company arrangement_ unless one but not both of the companies is an Australian

resident.

</dd> </dl></dl>

125-65  Meanings of demerger group, head entity and demerger subsidiary

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A _demerger group_ comprises the <sup>*</sup>head entity of

the group and one or more <sup>*</sup>demerger subsidiaries.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	An entity may be a member of one or more demerger groups.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A trust cannot be a member of a _demerger group_ unless

<sup>*</sup>CGT event E4 is capable of applying to all of the units and

interests in the trust.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	A discretionary trust cannot be a member of a demerger

group.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A company or trust is the _head entity_ of a

<sup>*</sup>demerger group if no other member of the group owns

<sup>*</sup>ownership interests in the company or trust.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>If apart from this subsection, a company or trust would be the <sup>*</sup>head entity of a <sup>*</sup>demerger group and the company or trust, and all of its <sup>*</sup>demerger subsidiaries, are also demerger subsidiaries of another company or trust in another demerger group, the first-mentioned company or trust is not the _head entity_ of a demerger group.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>A company or trust (the _first company or trust_) that would, apart from this subsection, be a member of a _demerger group_ is not a member of the _demerger group_ if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the first company or trust owns, either alone or together with another

company or trust that would, apart from this subsection, be a member of the

<sup>*</sup>demerger group, more than 20% but less than 80% of the

<sup>*</sup>ownership interests in a <sup>*</sup>listed public company or

<sup>*</sup>listed widely held trust; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the listed public company or listed widely held trust chooses that the

first company or trust not be a member of the demerger group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A company is a _demerger subsidiary_ of another company or a

trust that is a member of a <sup>*</sup>demerger group if the other company or

the trust, either alone or together with other members of the group, owns, or

has the right to <sup>*</sup>acquire, <sup>*</sup>ownership interests in the

company that carry between them:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the right to receive more than 20% of any distribution of income or

capital by the company; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the right to exercise, or control the exercise of, more than 20% of the

voting power of the company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>A trust is a _demerger subsidiary_ of another trust or a

company that is a member of a <sup>*</sup>demerger group if the other trust or

the company, either alone or together with other members of the group, owns, or

has the right to <sup>*</sup>acquire, <sup>*</sup>ownership interests in the

trust that carry between them the right to receive more than 20% of any

distribution of income or capital by the trustee.

</dd> </dl></dl>

125-70  Meanings of demerger, demerged entity and demerging entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A _demerger_ happens to a <sup>*</sup>demerger group if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>there is a restructuring of the demerger group; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>under the restructuring:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>members of the demerger group <sup>*</sup>dispose of at least 80% of their

total <sup>*</sup>ownership interests in another member of the demerger group

to owners of original interests in the <sup>*</sup>head entity of the demerger

group; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>at least 80% of the total ownership interests of members of the demerger

group in another member of the demerger group end and new interests are issued

to owners of original interests in the head entity; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the demerged entity issues sufficient new ownership interests in itself

with the result that owners of original interests in the head entity own at

least 80% of the total ownership interests in the demerged entity; or</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>some combination of the processes referred to in subparagraphs&#160;(i),

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>and (iii) happens with the effect that members of the demerger group stop

owning at least 80% of the total ownership interests owned by members of the

demerger group in another member of the group; and

</dd></dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

Note:	CGT event C2 and CGT event C3 are the only relevant CGT events in a subparagraph&#160;(ii) case.

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>under the restructuring:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>CGT event happens to an original interest owned by an entity

in the head entity of the group and the entity <sup>*</sup>acquires a new

interest and nothing else; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>no CGT event happens to an original interest owned by an entity in the

head entity of the group and the entity acquires a new interest and nothing

else; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the acquisition by entities of new interests happens only because those

entities own or owned original interests; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the new interests acquired are:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the head entity is a company&#151;ownership interests in a company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if the head entity is a trust&#151;ownership interests in a trust; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>just before the restructuring, it is reasonable for the head entity to

assume that more than 50% of original interests in the head entity of the

demerger group are owned by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>Australian residents; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>foreign residents whose new interests have the <sup>*</sup>necessary

connection with Australia just after they acquire them; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>neither the original interests nor the new interests are in a trust that

is a <sup>*</sup>superannuation fund; and</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>the requirements of subsection&#160;(2) are met.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Example:	To continue the example from subsection 125-55(1), Peter

owns 400 post-CGT shares in Company A. Companies A and B are both members of a

demerger group. Company A is the head entity of the demerger group and Company

B is a demerger subsidiary. 	Company A proceeds to demerge 100% of its shares in Company B to its shareholders. 	Company A enters into a proportionate capital reduction, returning 40 cents per share to its ordinary shareholders. Peter is entitled to $160 (40c times 400 shares) under the capital reduction. 	For Peter, the capital reduction amount of $160 is compulsorily applied to acquire Company A's shares in Company B, at $6.75 (a discount of 10% to current market value). Company A rounds up the fractional amounts in calculating the number of whole shares to be distributed to each shareholder. This gives Peter 24 shares in Company B (160 divided by 6.75, rounded up to the nearest whole number). Note:	Acquiring new interests by an owner of original interests may include the allocation of the owner's entitlement to new interests to a nominee:  </dl></dl>

*	to sell on the owner's behalf; or
 *	to hold pending the owner being located.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Each owner (an _original owner_) of original interests in the

<sup>*</sup>head entity of the <sup>*</sup>demerger group must:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>acquire, under the <sup>*</sup>demerger, the same proportion,

or as nearly as practicable the same proportion, of new interests in the

<sup>*</sup>demerged entity as the original owner owned in the head entity just

before the demerger; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>just after the demerger, have the same proportionate total

<sup>*</sup>market value of <sup>*</sup>ownership interests in the head entity

and demerged entity as the original owner owned in the head entity just before

the demerger.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	There is an exception: see section&#160;125-75\. Note 2:	Dual listed company voting shares are not treated as ownership interests: see section&#160;125-60\. Note 3:	Fractional interests will generally not affect your ability to choose a roll-over. Example:	To continue the example from subsection&#160;(1), Company A concludes, given the circumstances of the demerger, that the market values of Peter's and the other shareholders' shares in A and B are expected to be in proportion with their original interests in Company A, and advises the shareholders of this position.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In working out whether an original owner complies with subsection&#160;(2):

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>disregard <sup>*</sup>ownership interests that are original interests the

owner owns in the <sup>*</sup>demerged entity; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an anticipated reasonable approximation of the <sup>*</sup>market value of

ownership interests is sufficient.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Example:	An anticipated reasonable approximation of market values

of ownership interests may include:

 </dl></dl>

*	valuations provided to shareholders in scheme documents;
 *	the price selected for use under a sale facility;

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

	and may be made by reference to long-term value.

 </dl></dl>

_Exception: off-market buy-backs_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A buy-back of <sup>*</sup>shares that is an off-market purchase for the

purposes of Division&#160;16K of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ is not a <sup>*</sup>demerger.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Exception: roll-over available under another provision_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>Circumstances where an owner of original interests can obtain a roll-over

under a provision of this Act outside this Division for all of the CGT events

that happened to the owner's original interests under the circumstances cannot

be a _demerger_.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	An owner might be able to obtain a roll-over for the CGT

events under Subdivision&#160;124-E, 124-G, 124-H or 124-M.

 </dl></dl>

_Meaning of demerged entity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>An entity that is a former member of a <sup>*</sup>demerger group is a

_demerged entity_ if, under a <sup>*</sup>demerger that happens to

the group, <sup>*</sup>ownership interests in the entity are acquired by:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>shareholders in the <sup>*</sup>head entity of the group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>unitholders or holders of interests in the head entity of the group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Meaning of demerging entity_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>An entity that is a member of a <sup>*</sup>demerger group just before the

<sup>*</sup>CGT event referred to in section&#160;125-155 happens is a

_demerging entity_ if, under a <sup>*</sup>demerger that happens to

the group:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the entity (either alone or together with other members of the demerger

group)<sup>*</sup>dispose of at least 80% of their total <sup>*</sup>ownership

interests in another member of the demerger group to owners of original

interests in the <sup>*</sup>head entity of the demerger group; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at least 80% of the total ownership interests of that entity and of other

members of the demerger group in another member of the demerger group end and

new interests are issued to owners of original interests in the head entity; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Note:	CGT event C2 and CGT event C3 are the only relevant CGT events.

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the demerged entity issues sufficient new ownership interests in itself

with the result that owners of original interests in the head entity own at

least 80% of the total ownership interests in the demerged entity; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>some combination of the processes referred to in paragraphs&#160;(a), (b)

and (c) happens with the effect that members of the demerger group stop owning

at least 80% of the total ownership interests owned by members of the demerger

group in another member of the group.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

125-75  Exceptions to subsection 125-70(2)

_Employee share schemes_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>In working out whether the requirements in subsection 125-70(2) are met,

disregard each of the <sup>*</sup>ownership interests described in

subsections&#160;(2) and (3) if, just before the <sup>*</sup>demerger, those

interests (taking into account either or both of their number and value)

represented not more than 3% of the total <sup>*</sup>ownership interests in

the entity.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>ownership interest in a company that is owned by an entity is disregarded under subsection&#160;(1) if the ownership interest: </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>qualifying share or a <sup>*</sup>qualifying right

<sup>*</sup>acquired under an <sup>*</sup>employee share scheme; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>share acquired under a <sup>*</sup>scheme to which

section&#160;26AAC of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is not a fully-paid ordinary share.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>ownership interest in a trust that is owned by an entity is

disregarded under subsection&#160;(1) if the ownership interest:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>would be a <sup>*</sup>qualifying share or a <sup>*</sup>qualifying right

<sup>*</sup>acquired under an <sup>*</sup>employee share scheme if

Division&#160;13A of Part&#160;III of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_

applied to ownership interests in a trust; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is not a fully-paid unit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Adjusting instruments_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>In working out whether the requirements in subsection 125-70(2) are met,

disregard each of the <sup>*</sup>ownership interests described in

subsection&#160;(5) (_adjusting instruments_) if, just before the

<sup>*</sup>demerger, those interests represented not more than 10%, or such

greater percentage (not exceeding 17%) as is prescribed, of the ownership

interests in the entity.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>An <sup>*</sup>ownership interest in a <sup>*</sup>listed public company or a <sup>*</sup>listed widely held trust that is the <sup>*</sup>head entity of a <sup>*</sup>demerger group is disregarded under subsection&#160;(4) if: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the adjusting instrument was issued on terms that ensure that its value is

not adversely affected by an <sup>*</sup>arrangement undertaken by the company

or trust in relation to other ownership interests in the company or trust;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the adjusting instrument can be converted into an ordinary

<sup>*</sup>share in the company or an ordinary unit in the trust, any

conversion will occur on a basis:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>that is set out in the terms of the issue of the instrument; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>that is adjusted to take into account a capital reduction or a capital

reconstruction; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>before conversion, the owner of the adjusting instrument does not have a

right to participate in distributions of profit or capital except as set out in

the terms of the issue of the instrument; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the adjusting instrument deals with the effect of a <sup>*</sup>demerger

that happens to the demerger group on the value of the instrument.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Example:	Some examples of adjusting instruments are:

 </dl></dl>

*	convertible preference shares, including reset preference shares;
 *	convertible notes;
 *	partly paid shares where the paid-up amount is adjusted to reflect a capital reduction.

_Additional exceptions_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The regulations may provide that, in working out whether the requirements

in subsection 125-70(2) are met, other <sup>*</sup>ownership interests of a

kind specified in the regulations are to be disregarded if, just before the

<sup>*</sup>demerger, those interests represented not more than a prescribed

percentage of the ownership interests in the entity.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>However, the total percentage of <sup>*</sup>ownership interests to be disregarded under this section must not exceed 20% of the ownership interests in the entity. </dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

125-80  What is the roll-over?

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If you choose the roll-over, a <sup>*</sup>capital gain or

<sup>*</sup>capital loss you make from a <sup>*</sup>CGT event happening under

the <sup>*</sup>demerger to an original interest you own is disregarded.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If you choose the roll-over, the first element of the <sup>*</sup>cost base and <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each new interest that you are not taken to have <sup>*</sup>acquired

before 20&#160;September 1985; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if not all of your original interests ended under the

<sup>*</sup>demerger&#151;each of your remaining original interests that you

acquired on or after 20&#160;September 1985;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

is such proportion of the sum of the cost bases of all your original interests that you acquired on or after 20&#160;September 1985 (worked out just before the demerger) as is reasonable having regard to the matters specified in subsection&#160;(3).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	These rules replace the cost base and reduced cost base

adjustments in CGT event E4 and CGT event G1\. Note 2:	The head entity or the demerging entity may advise you of the proportions.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The matters are:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>market values of your remaining original interests just

after the <sup>*</sup>demerger, or an anticipated reasonable approximation of

those market values; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the market values of your new interests just after the demerger, or an

anticipated reasonable approximation of those market values.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Example:	To continue the example from subsection 125-70(2),

Company A advises its shareholders that Company B at that time represents 5% of

the market value of the group as a whole. Peter's cost base for each of his

shares in A is $4.60, and Peter recalculates his cost base as follows:

 </dl></dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1227.gif)</sub>

to be spread over 400 shares in A and 24 shares in B.

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1228.gif)</sub>
 <sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1229.gif)</sub>
 <sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1230.gif)</sub>
 <sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01281/Html/9EF1056E86D3C5ACCA256F710056BC4B/$FILE/1231.gif)</sub>

_Pre-CGT interests_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The following subsections apply if you choose the roll-over and you

<sup>*</sup>acquired some or all of your original interests before

20&#160;September 1985.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If you <sup>*</sup>acquired all of your original interests before 20&#160;September 1985, you are taken to have acquired all of your new interests before that day.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>If you <sup>*</sup>acquired some of your original interests before 20&#160;September 1985, you are taken to have acquired a reasonable whole number of your new interests before that day having regard to: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>market values of your original interests and your

remaining original interests just after the <sup>*</sup>demerger, or an

anticipated reasonable approximation of those market values; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the market values of your new interests just after the demerger, or an

anticipated reasonable approximation of those market values.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>If a proportion, but not all of, your original interests ends under the

<sup>*</sup>demerger and you <sup>*</sup>acquired some of your original

interests before 20&#160;September 1985, that same proportion of those

interests you acquired before that day ends.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	CGT event K6 may be relevant if you later dispose your

interests that are treated as being pre-CGT. Example:	Bert owned 100 shares in a company of which 50 were acquired pre-CGT. Under a demerger 20 of Bert's 100 shares were cancelled in exchange for new interests. As 20% of his shares were cancelled, 10 of his pre-CGT shares are taken to have been cancelled.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>If you choose a roll-over for some but not all of your original interests,

you apply the rules in this section as if your original interests for which you

chose the roll-over were your only original interests.

</dd> </dl></dl>

125-85  Cost base adjustments where CGT event happens but no roll-over chosen

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>You must adjust the <sup>*</sup>cost base and <sup>*</sup>reduced cost

base of an <sup>*</sup>ownership interest you own in a company or trust if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>demerger happens to a <sup>*</sup>demerger group of which

the company or trust is a member; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>you owned an original interest in the <sup>*</sup>head entity of the

demerger group just before the demerger; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>CGT event happens to the original interest and you

<sup>*</sup>acquire a new interest under the demerger; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>you do not choose a roll-over under this Subdivision for the original

interest.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The adjustments you must make are the same as the adjustments you would

have to make under section&#160;125-80 for the <sup>*</sup>cost bases and

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost bases of the remaining original interests and new

interests just after the <sup>*</sup>CGT event if you could have chosen a

roll-over under this Subdivision for the <sup>*</sup>demerger and you had done

so.

</dd> </dl></dl>

125-90  Cost base adjustments where no CGT event

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>You must adjust the <sup>*</sup>cost base and <sup>*</sup>reduced cost

base of an <sup>*</sup>ownership interest you own in a company or trust if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a <sup>*</sup>demerger happens to a <sup>*</sup>demerger group of which

the company or trust is a member; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>you owned an original interest in the <sup>*</sup>head entity of the

demerger group just before the demerger; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>no <sup>*</sup>CGT event happens to the original interest, but you

<sup>*</sup>acquire a new interest under the demerger.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The adjustments you must make are the same as the adjustments you would

have to make under section&#160;125-80 if you could have chosen a roll-over

under this Subdivision for the <sup>*</sup>demerger and you had done so.

</dd> </dl></dl>

125-95  No other cost base adjustment after demerger

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		If you have to make adjustments to the <sup>*</sup>cost base and

<sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of your <sup>*</sup>ownership interests under

section&#160;125-80, 125-85 or 125-90 because of a <sup>*</sup>demerger, no

other adjustment can be made under this Act to those cost bases and reduced

cost bases because of something that happens under the demerger.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Those sections deal with any value shift that might occur

under the demerger and avoid the need for the general value shifting regime to

apply.

 </dl></dl>

125-100  No further demerger relief in some cases

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		This Division does not apply to the remaining <sup>*</sup>ownership interests

in a <sup>*</sup>demerged entity if one or more members of the

<sup>*</sup>demerger group <sup>*</sup>disposed of or cancelled less than 100%

of the total ownership interests of that group in the demerged entity.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	After the demerger, a former member of the demerger group

can undertake a further demerger to which this Division can apply.

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;125-C&#151;Consequences for members of demerger group
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;125-C
 125-150  Guide to Subdivision&#160;125-C

Certain capital gains and capital losses that members of a demerger group make under a demerger are disregarded.
 Certain capital losses made under a demerger are reduced where the demerger results in a value shift.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

125-155	Certain capital gains or losses disregarded for demerging entity
 125-160	No CGT event J1
 125-165	Adjusted capital loss for value shift under a demerger
 125-170	Reduced cost base reduction if demerger asset subject to roll-over

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 125-155  Certain capital gains or losses disregarded for demerging entity

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		Any <sup>*</sup>capital gain or <sup>*</sup>capital loss a

<sup>*</sup>demerging entity makes from <sup>*</sup>CGT event A1,

<sup>*</sup>CGT event C2, <sup>*</sup>CGT event C3 or <sup>*</sup>CGT event K6

happening to its <sup>*</sup>ownership interests in a <sup>*</sup>demerged

entity under a <sup>*</sup>demerger is disregarded.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	The full list of CGT events is in section&#160;104-5\. Note 2:	This section will not apply if section&#160;125-100 applies.  </dl></dl>

125-160  No CGT event J1

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		<sup>*</sup>CGT event J1 does not happen to a <sup>*</sup>demerged entity or

a member of a <sup>*</sup>demerger group under a <sup>*</sup>demerger.

 </dl></dl>

125-165  Adjusted capital loss for value shift under a demerger

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		A <sup>*</sup>capital loss made by an entity that was a member of a

<sup>*</sup>demerger group from a <sup>*</sup>CGT event happening to a

<sup>*</sup>CGT asset under a <sup>*</sup>demerger or after a demerger is

reduced to the extent that the capital loss is reasonably attributable to a

reduction in the <sup>*</sup>market value of the asset because of the demerger.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Example:	The market value of equity or loan interests in the

demerging entity may be reduced by the disposal, for inadequate value, of

ownership interests of another member of the demerger group to owners of

original interests in the head entity of the group.

 </dl></dl>

125-170  Reduced cost base reduction if demerger asset subject to roll-over

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset is reduced if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the <sup>*</sup>market value of the asset is reduced because of a

<sup>*</sup>demerger; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>after the demerger the asset is <sup>*</sup>acquired by an entity from

another entity (the _transferor_) in a situation where the

transferor obtained a roll-over for the disposal; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the reduction occurred when the transferor owned the asset.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of the asset as determined under the

roll-over is reduced just after the roll-over to the extent of the reduction in

<sup>*</sup>market value caused by the <sup>*</sup>demerger.

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The rules in section&#160;125-165 and this section deal

with any value shift that might occur under the demerger and avoid the need for

the general value shifting regime to apply.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the <sup>*</sup>reduced cost base of a <sup>*</sup>CGT asset is reduced

under this section because of a <sup>*</sup>demerger, no other adjustment can

be made under this Act to that reduced cost base because of something that

happens under the demerger.

</dd> </dl></dl>

Subdivision&#160;125-D&#151;Corporate unit trusts and public trading trusts
 Guide to Subdivision&#160;125-D
 125-225  Guide to Subdivision&#160;125-D

This Division applies to corporate unit trusts and public trading trusts as if they were companies.

Table of sections

Operative provisions

125-230	Application of Division to corporate unit trusts and public trading trusts

_\[This is the end of the Guide.]_

Operative provisions
 125-230  Application of Division to corporate unit trusts and public trading trusts

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		This Division applies to a trust to which section&#160;102K or 102S of the

_Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ applies for an income year in which a

<sup>*</sup>demerger happens as if:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the trust were a company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd><sup>*</sup>ownership interests in it were interests in a company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

10  At the end of section&#160;44

Add:

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsections&#160;(3) and (4) apply to a demerger dividend unless the head

entity elects in writing, within one month after it decides which of its

shareholders will receive ownership interests in the demerged entity under the

demerger, that those subsections do not apply to the total demerger dividend

for all shareholders.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>This section applies to the demerger dividend as if it had not been paid out of profits.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>A demerger dividend is not assessable income or exempt income.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>However, subsections&#160;(3) and (4) do not apply to a demerger dividend unless, just after the demerger, CGT assets owned by the demerged entity or a demerger subsidiary representing at least 50% by market value of all the CGT assets (or a reasonable approximation of market value) owned by the demerged entity and its demerger subsidiaries are used, directly or indirectly, in one or more businesses carried on by one or more of those entities.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>In applying subsection&#160;(5), disregard any assets that are ownership interests in a demerger subsidiary unless they are used in a business referred to in that subsection. </dd> </dl></dl>

11  Section&#160;45B

Repeal the section, substitute:

45B  Schemes to provide certain benefits

_Purpose of section_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The purpose of this section is to ensure that relevant amounts are treated

as dividends for taxation purposes if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>components of a demerger allocation as between capital and profit do not

reflect the circumstances of a demerger; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>certain payments, allocations and distributions are made in substitution

for dividends.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Application of section_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section applies if:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>there is a scheme under which a person is provided with a demerger benefit

or a capital benefit by a company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>under the scheme, a taxpayer (the _relevant taxpayer_), who

may or may not be the person provided with the demerger benefit or the capital

benefit, obtains a tax benefit; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>having regard to the relevant circumstances of the scheme, it would be

concluded that the person, or one of the persons, who entered into or carried

out the scheme or any part of the scheme did so for a purpose (whether or not

the dominant purpose but not including an incidental purpose) of enabling a

taxpayer (the _relevant taxpayer_) to obtain a tax benefit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Commissioner to determine that sectionÂ 45BA o_ r _45C applies_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Commissioner may make, in writing, a determination that:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section&#160;45BA applies in relation to the whole, or a part, of the

demerger benefit; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section&#160;45C applies in relation to the whole, or a part, of the

capital benefit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

A determination does not form part of an assessment.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If section&#160;45BA applies in relation to the whole, or a

part, of a demerger benefit, this benefit may be a capital benefit.

 </dl></dl>

_Meaning of provided with a demerger benefit_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A person is _provided with a demerger benefit_ if in relation

to a demerger:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a company provides the person with ownership interests in that or another

company; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>something is done in relation to an ownership interest owned by the person

that has the effect of increasing the value of an ownership interest (which may

or may not be the same ownership interest) owned by the person.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Meaning of provided with a capital benefit_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A reference to a person being _provided with a capital benefit_ is a reference to any of the following:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the provision of ownership interests in a company to the person;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the distribution to the person of share capital or share premium;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>something that is done in relation to an ownership interest that has the

effect of increasing the value of an ownership interest (which may or may not

be the same interest) that is held by the person.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>However, a person is not _provided with a capital benefit_ to

the extent that the provision of interests, the distribution or the thing done

referred to in subsection&#160;(5) involves the person receiving a demerger

dividend.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, a non-share distribution to an equity holder is taken to be the distribution to the equity holder of share capital to the extent to which it is a non-share capital return. </dd> </dl></dl>

_Meaning of relevant circumstances of scheme_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>The _relevant circumstances_ of a scheme include:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the extent to which the demerger benefit or capital benefit is

attributable to capital or the extent to which the demerger benefit or capital

benefit is attributable to profits (realised and unrealised) of the company or

of an associate (within the meaning in section&#160;318) of the company;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the pattern of distributions of dividends, bonus shares and returns of

capital or share premium by the company or by an associate (within the meaning

in section&#160;318) of the company;</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>whether the relevant taxpayer has capital losses that, apart from the

scheme, would be carried forward to a later year of income;</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>whether some or all of the ownership interests in the company or in an

associate (within the meaning in section&#160;318) of the company held by the

relevant taxpayer were acquired, or are taken to have been acquired, by the

relevant taxpayer before 20&#160;September 1985;</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>whether the relevant taxpayer is a non-resident;</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>whether the cost base (for the purposes of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1997_) of the relevant ownership interest is not substantially less than

the value of the applicable demerger benefit or capital benefit;</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>whether the relevant taxpayer or an associate (within the meaning in

section&#160;318) of the taxpayer is a private company that would not have been

entitled to a rebate under section&#160;46F if the taxpayer had been paid an

equivalent dividend instead of the demerger benefit or capital benefit;</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>if the scheme involves the distribution of share capital or share

premium&#151;whether the interest held by the relevant taxpayer after the

distribution is the same as the interest would have been if an equivalent

dividend had been paid instead of the distribution of share capital or share

premium;</dd>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the scheme involves the provision of ownership interests and the later

disposal of those interests, or an increase in the value of ownership interests

and the later disposal of those interests:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the period for which the ownership interests are held by the holder of the

interests; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>when the arrangement for the disposal of the ownership interests was

entered into;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>for a demerger only:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>whether the profits of the demerging entity and demerged entity are

attributable to transactions between the entity and an associate (within the

meaning in section&#160;318) of the entity; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>whether the assets of the demerging entity and demerged entity were

acquired under transactions between the entity and an associate (within the

meaning in section&#160;318) of the entity;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(k)</dt><dd>any of the matters referred to in subparagraphs 177D(b)(i) to (viii).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Meaning of obtaining a tax benefit_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>A relevant taxpayer _obtains a tax benefit_ if an amount of

tax payable, or any other amount payable under this Act, by the relevant

taxpayer would, apart from this section, be less than the amount that would

have been payable, or would be payable at a later time than it would have been

payable, if the demerger benefit had been an assessable dividend or the capital

benefit had been a dividend.

</dd> </dl></dl>

_Expressions to have same meanings as in PartÂ IIIAA_

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(10)</dt><dd>Expressions used in this section that are defined in Part&#160;IIIAA have

the same meanings as in that Part.

</dd> </dl></dl>

45BA  Effect of determinations under section&#160;45B for demerger benefits

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the Commissioner makes a determination under subsection 45B(3), the

amount of the demerger benefit, or the part of the benefit, is taken not to be

a demerger dividend for the purposes of this Act for the owner of the ownership

interest or the relevant taxpayer at the time when the owner or relevant

taxpayer is provided with the demerger benefit.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The amount of the demerger benefit is: </dd> </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the benefit is the provision of an ownership interest&#151;the market value

of the interest at the time that it is provided; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the benefit is an increase in the value of an ownership interest&#151;the

increase in the market value of the interest as a result of the change; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the benefit is a distribution to the shareholder of share capital or

share premium&#151;the amount debited to the share capital account or share premium

account of the company in connection with the provision of the benefit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

45C  Effect of determinations under sections&#160;45A and 45B for capital benefits
 13  Subsection 45C(4)

15  Paragraphs 45C(4)(a) and (b)

45C, the Commissioner must give a copy of the determination to the company

concerned (which, in the case of a demerger benefit referred to in

section&#160;45B, is the head entity of the demerger group). The notice may be

included in a notice of assessment.

</dd> </dl></dl>

or 45B, give a copy of the notice to:

</dd> </dl></dl>

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the advantaged shareholder referred to in section&#160;45A; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the relevant taxpayer referred to in section&#160;45B.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part&#160;4&#151;Transitional
 54  Transitional

A company that makes payments in respect of shares in the company under a demerger that happens on or after 1&#160;July 2002 and before this Act receives the Royal Assent can choose to apply section&#160;45B of the _Income Tax Assessment Act 1936_ as that section existed before the amendments made by this Act to the demerger rather than that section as amended by this Act if:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the head entity of the demerger group is a listed public company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the only CGT events (if any) that happen under the demerger to all

original interests in that head entity are CGT event A1, CGT event C2 or CGT

event G1.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part&#160;5&#151;Application
 55  Application

The amendments made by this Schedule apply to demergers happening on or after 1&#160;July 2002.
